#Text:Kauśikasūtra
#Edition:Bloomfield (DCS version)



1.1.1	atha vidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
1.1.2	sa punar āmnāyapratyayaḥ
1.1.3	āmnāyaḥ punar mantrāś ca brāhmaṇāni ca
1.1.4	tad yathābrāhmaṇaṃ vidhir evaṃ karmaliṅgā mantrāḥ
1.1.5	tathānyārthaḥ
1.1.6	tathā brāhmaṇaliṅgā mantrāḥ
1.1.7	tadabhāve saṃpradāyaḥ
1.1.8	pramuktatvād brāhmaṇānām
1.1.9	yajñaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
1.1.10	devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca
1.1.11	prāṅmukha upāṃśu karoti
1.1.12	yajñopavītī devānām
1.1.13	prācīnavītī pitṝṇām
1.1.14	prāg udag vā devānām
1.1.15	dakṣiṇā pitṝṇām
1.1.16	prāgudagapavargaṃ devānām
1.1.17	dakṣiṇāpratyagapavargaṃ pitṝṇām
1.1.18	sakṛt karma pitṝṇām
1.1.19	tryavarārdhaṃ devānām
1.1.20	yathādiṣṭaṃ vā
1.1.21	abhidakṣiṇam ācāro devānām
1.1.22	prasavyaṃ pitṝṇām
1.1.23	svāhākāravaṣaṭkārapradānā devāḥ
1.1.24	svadhākāranamaskārapradānā pitaraḥ
1.1.25	upamūlalūnaṃ barhiḥ pitṝṇām
1.1.26	parvasu devānām
1.1.27	pra yaccha parśum iti darbhāhārāya dātraṃ prayacchati
1.1.28	oṣadhīr dāntu parvan ityupari parvaṇāṃ lūtvā tūṣṇīm āhṛtyottarato 'gner upasādayati
1.1.29	nāgniṃ viparyāvarteta
1.1.30	nāntarā yajñāṅgāni vyaveyāt
1.1.31	dakṣiṇaṃ jānu prabhujya juhoti
1.1.32	yā pūrvā paurṇamāsī sānumatir yottarā sā rākā
1.1.33	yā pūrvāmāvāsyā sā sinīvālī yottarā sā kuhūḥ
1.1.34	adyopavasatha ityupavatsyadbhaktam aśnāti
1.1.35	madhulavaṇamāṃsamāṣavarjam
1.1.36	mamāgne varcaḥ iti samidha ādhāya vratam upaiti
1.1.37	vratena tvāṃ vratapate iti vā
1.1.38	brahmacārī vratī
1.1.39	adhaḥ śayīta
1.1.40	prātarhute 'gnau karmaṇe vāṃ veṣāya vāṃ sukṛtāya vām iti pāṇī prakṣālyāpareṇāgner darbhān āstīrya teṣūttaram ānaḍuhaṃ rohitaṃ carma prāggrīvam uttaraloma prastīrya pavitre kurute
1.1.41	darbhāvaprachinnāntau prakṣālyānulomam anumārṣṭi viṣṇor manasā pūte sthaḥ iti
1.2.1	tvaṃ bhūmim aty eṣy ojasā tvaṃ vedyāṃ sīdasi cārur adhvare tvāṃ pavitram ṛṣayo bharantas tvaṃ punīhi duritāny asmat iti pavitre antardhāya havir nirvapati devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi iti
1.2.2	evam agniṣomābhyām iti
1.2.3	indrāgnibhyām ityamāvāsyāyām
1.2.4	nityaṃ pūrvam āgneyam
1.2.5	niruptaṃ pavitrābhyāṃ prokṣati amuṣmai tvā juṣṭam yathādevatam
1.2.6	ulūkhalamusalaṃ śūrpaṃ prakṣālitaṃ carmaṇyādhāya vrīhīn ulūkhala opyāvaghnaṃs trir haviṣkṛtā vācaṃ visṛjati haviṣkṛd ā dravehi iti
1.2.7	avahatya suphalīkṛtān kṛtvā triḥ prakṣālya taṇḍulān agne varur yajñiyas tvādhi arukṣat iti carum adhidadhāti
1.2.8	śuddhāḥ pūtāḥ ityudakam āsiñcati
1.2.9	brahmaṇā śuddhāḥ iti taṇḍulān
1.2.10	pari tvāgne puraṃ vayam iti triḥ paryagni karoti
1.2.11	nekṣaṇena triḥ pradakṣiṇam udāyauti
1.2.12	ata ūrdhvaṃ yathākāmam
1.2.13	uttarato 'gner upasādayatīdhmam
1.2.14	uttaraṃ barhiḥ
1.2.15	agnaye tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi itīdhmam
1.2.16	pṛthivyai iti barhiḥ
1.2.17	darbhamuṣṭim abhyukṣya paścād agneḥ prāgagraṃ nidadhāti ūrṇamradaṃ prathasva svāsasthaṃ devebhyaḥ iti
1.2.18	darbhāṇām apādāya ṛṣīṇāṃ prastaro 'si iti dakṣiṇato 'gner brahmāsanaṃ nidadhāti
1.2.19	purastād agner āstīrya teṣāṃ mūlānyapareṣāṃ prāntair avacchādayan parisarpati dakṣiṇenāgnim ā paścārdhāt
1.2.20	pari stṛṇīhi iti sampreṣyati
1.2.21	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ prasūtaḥ praśiṣā paristṛṇāmi iti
1.2.22	evam uttarato 'yujo dhātūn kurvan
1.2.23	yatra samāgacchanti tad dakṣiṇottaraṃ kṛṇoti
1.2.24	stīrṇaṃ prokṣati haviṣāṃ tvā juṣṭaṃ prokṣāmi iti
1.2.25	nānabhyukṣitaṃ saṃstīrṇam upayogaṃ labheta
1.2.26	naidho'bhyādānam
1.2.27	nānutpūtaṃ haviḥ
1.2.28	nāprokṣitaṃ yajñāṅgam
1.2.29	tasmin prakṣālitopavātāni nidadhāti
1.2.30	sruvam ājyadhānīṃ ca
1.2.31	vilīnapūtam ājyaṃ gṛhītvādhiśritya paryagni kṛtvodag udvāsya paścād agner upasādyodagagrābhyāṃ pavitrābhyām utpunāti
1.2.32	viṣṇor manasā pūtam asi
1.2.33	devas tvā savitot punātu
1.2.34	acchidreṇa tvā pavitreṇa śatadhāreṇa sahasradhāreṇa supvot punāmi iti tṛtīyam
1.2.35	tūṣṇīṃ caturtham
1.2.36	śṛtaṃ havir abhighārayati madhvā samañjan ghṛtavat karātha iti
1.2.37	abhighāryodañcam udvāsayati ud vāsayāgneḥ śṛtam akarma havyam ā sīda pṛṣṭham amṛtasya dhāma iti
1.2.38	paścād ājyasya nidhāyālaṃkṛtya samānenotpunāti
1.2.39	adārasṛt ityavekṣate
1.2.40	ut tiṣṭhata ityaindram
1.2.41	agnir bhūyām iti tisṛbhir upasamādadhāti asmai kṣatrāṇi etam idhmam iti vā
1.3.1	yunajmi tvā brahmaṇā daivyena havyāyāsmai voḍheva jātavedaḥ indhānās tvā suprajasaḥ suvīrā jyog jīvema balihṛto vayaṃ te iti
1.3.2	dakṣiṇato jāṅmāyanam udapātram upasādyābhimantrayate tathodapātraṃ dhāraya yathāgre brahmaṇaspatiḥ satyadharmā adīdharad devasya savituḥ save iti
1.3.3	athodakam āsiñcati iheta devīr amṛtaṃ vasānā hiraṇyavarṇā anavadyarūpāḥ āpaḥ samudro varuṇaś ca rājā saṃpātabhāgān haviṣo juṣantām indrapraśiṣṭā varuṇaprasūtā apaḥ samudrād divam ud vahantu indrapraśiṣṭā varuṇaprasūtā divas pṛthivyā śriyam ud vahantu iti
1.3.4	ṛtaṃ tvā satyena pariṣiñcāmi jātavedaḥ iti saha havirbhiḥ paryukṣya jīvābhir ācamyotthāya vedaprapadbhiḥ prapadyata oṃ prapadye bhūḥ prapadye bhuvaḥ prapadye svaḥ prapadye janat prapadye iti
1.3.5	prapadya paścāt stīrṇasya darbhān āstīrya ahe daidhiṣavyod atas tiṣṭhāny asya sadane sīda yo 'smat pākatara iti brahmāsanam anvīkṣate
1.3.6	nirastaḥ parāgvasuḥ saha pāpmanā nirastaḥ so 'stu yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti dakṣiṇā tṛṇaṃ nirasyati
1.3.7	tad anvālabhya japati idam aham arvāgvasoḥ sadane sīdāmyṛtasya sadane sīdāmi satyasya sadane sīdāmīṣṭasya sadane sīdāmi pūrtasya sadane sīdāmi māmṛṣad deva barhiḥ svāsasthaṃ tvādhyāsadeyam ūrṇamradam anabhiśokam
1.3.8	vimṛgvarīṃ ityupaviśyāsanīyaṃ brahmajapaṃ japati bṛhaspatir brahmā brahmasadana āsiṣyate bṛhaspate yajñaṃ gopāya yad ud udvata un nivataḥ śakeyam iti
1.3.9	darbhaiḥ sruvaṃ nirmṛjya niṣṭaptaṃ rakṣo niṣṭaptā arātayaḥ pratyuṣṭaṃ rakṣaḥ pratyuṣṭā arātayaḥ iti pratapya mūle sruvaṃ gṛhītvā japati viṣṇor hasto 'si dakṣiṇaḥ pūṣṇā datto bṛhaspateḥ taṃ tvāhaṃ sruvam ā dade devānāṃ havyavāhanam ayaṃ sruvo vi dadhāti homān śatākṣarachandasā jāgatena sarvā yajñasya samanakti viṣṭhā bārhaspatyeṣṭiḥ śarmaṇā daivyena iti
1.3.10	oṃ bhūḥ śaṃ bhūtyai tvā gṛhṇe bhūtaye iti prathamaṃ grahaṃ gṛhṇāti
1.3.11	oṃ bhuvaḥ śaṃ puṣṭyai tvā gṛhṇe puṣṭaye iti dvitīyam
1.3.12	oṃ svaḥ śaṃ tvā gṛhṇe sahasrapoṣāya iti tṛtīyam
1.3.13	oṃ jagacchaṃ tvā gṛhṇe 'parimitapoṣāya iti caturtham
1.3.14	rājakarmābhicārikeṣu amuṣya tvā prāṇāya gṛhṇe 'pānāya vyānāya samānāyodānāya iti pañcamam
1.3.15	agnāv agniḥ hṛdā pūtam purastād yuktaḥ yajñasya cakṣuḥ iti juhoti
1.3.16	paścād agner madhyadeśe samānatra purastāddhomān
1.3.17	dakṣiṇenāgnim udapātra ājyāhutīnāṃ saṃpātān ānayati
1.3.18	purastāddhoma ājyabhāgaḥ saṃsthitahomaḥ samṛddhiḥ śāntānām
1.3.19	ityetāvājyabhāgau
1.4.1	vṛṣṇe bṛhate svarvide agnaye śulkaṃ harāmi tviṣīmate sa na sthirān balavataḥ kṛṇotu jyok ca no jīvātave dadhāti agnaye svāhā ityuttarapūrvārdha āgneyam ājyabhāgaṃ juhoti
1.4.2	dakṣiṇapūrvārdhe somāya tvaṃ soma divyo nṛcakṣāḥ sugāṁ asmabhyaṃ patho anu khyaḥ abhi no gotraṃ viduṣa iva neṣo 'cchā no vācam uśatīṃ jigāsi somāya svāhā iti
1.4.3	madhye haviḥ
1.4.4	upastīryājyaṃ saṃhatābhyām aṅgulibhyāṃ dvir haviṣo 'vadyati madhyāt pūrvārdhācca
1.4.5	avattam abhighārya dvir haviḥ pratyabhighārayati
1.4.6	yato yato 'vadyati tad anupūrvam
1.4.7	evaṃ sarvāṇyavadānāni
1.4.8	anyatra sauviṣṭakṛtāt
1.4.9	ud enam uttaraṃ naya iti purastāddhomasaṃhatāṃ pūrvām
1.4.10	evaṃ pūrvāṃ pūrvāṃ saṃhatāṃ juhoti
1.4.11	svāhāntābhiḥ pratyṛcaṃ homāḥ
1.4.12	yām uttarām agner ājyabhāgasya juhoti rakṣodevatyā sā yāṃ dakṣiṇataḥ somasya pitṛdevatyā sā
1.4.13	tasmād antarā hotavyā devaloka eva hūyante
1.4.14	yāṃ hutvā pūrvām aparāṃ juhoti sāpakramantī sa pāpīyān yajamāno bhavati
1.4.15	yāṃ parāṃ parāṃ saṃhatāṃ juhoti sābhikramantī sa vasīyān yajamāno bhavati
1.4.16	yām anagnau juhoti sāndhā tayā cakṣur yajamānasya mīyate so 'ndhaṃbhāvuko yajamāno bhavati
1.4.17	yāṃ dhūme juhoti sā tamasi hūyate so 'rocako yajamāno bhavati
1.4.18	yāṃ jyotiṣmati juhoti tayā brahmavarcasī bhavati tasmājjyotiṣmati hotavyam
1.4.19	evam asmai kṣatram agnīṣomau ityagniṣomīyasya
1.5.1	agnīṣomā savedasā sahūtī vanataṃ giraḥ sa devatrā babhūvathuḥ yuvam etāni divi rocanāny agniś ca soma sakratū adhattam yuvaṃ sindhūṃr abhiśaster avadyād agnīṣomāv amuñcataṃ gṛbhītān agnīṣomā ya āhutiṃ yo vāṃ dāśāddhaviṣkṛtim sa prajayā suvīryaṃ viśvam āyur vyaśnavat
1.5.2	indrāgnī rocanā divaḥ pari vājeṣu bhūṣathaḥ tad vāṃ ceti pra vīryam śnathad vṛtram uta sanoti vājam indrā yo agnī sahurī saparyāt irajyantā vasavyasya bhūreḥ sahastamā sahasā vājayantā indrāgnī asmān rakṣatāṃ yau prajānāṃ prajāvatī sa prajayā suvīryaṃ viśvam āyur vyaśnavat gomaddhiraṇyavad vasu yad vām aśvāvad īmahe indrāgnī vanemahi svāhā iti
1.5.3	aindrāgnasya haviṣo 'māvāsyāyām
1.5.4	prāk sviṣṭakṛtaḥ pārvaṇahomau samṛddhihomāḥ kāmyahomāś ca
1.5.5	pūrṇā paścāt iti paurṇamāsyām
1.5.6	yat te devā akṛṇvan bhāgadheyam ityamāvāsyāyām
1.5.7	ākūtyai tvā svāhā kāmāya tvā svāhā samṛdhe tvā svāhā ākūtyai tvā kāmāya tvā samṛdhe tvā svāhā ṛcā stomaṃ samardhaya gāyatreṇa rathantaraṃ bṛhad gāyatravartani svāhā
1.5.8	pṛthivyām agnaye samanaman iti saṃnatibhiś ca prajāpate na tvad etāny anyaḥ iti ca
1.5.9	upastīryājyaṃ sarveṣām uttarataḥ sakṛtsakṛd avadāya dvir avattam abhighārayati
1.5.10	na havīṃṣi
1.5.11	ā devānām api panthām aganma yacchaknavāma tad anupravoḍhum agnir vidvān sa yajāt sa iddhotā so 'dhvarān sa ṛtūn kalpayāti agnaye sviṣṭakṛte svāhā ity uttarapūrvārdhe 'vayutaṃ hutvā sarvaprāyaścittīyān homāñjuhoti
1.5.12	svāheṣṭebhyaḥ svāhā vaṣaḍ aniṣṭebhyaḥ svāhā bheṣajaṃ sviṣṭyai svāhā niṣkṛtir duriṣṭyai svāhā daivībhyas tanūbhyaḥ svāhā ayāś cāgne 'sy anabhiśastiś ca satyam it tvam ayā asi ayāsā manasā kṛto 'yās san havyam ūhiṣe ā no dhehi bheṣajam svāhā iti oṃ svāhā bhūḥ svāhā bhuvaḥ svāhā svaḥ svāhoṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā iti
1.6.1	yan me skannaṃ manaso jātavedo yad vāskandaddhaviṣo yatra yatra utpruṣo vipruṣaḥ saṃ juhomi satyāḥ santu yajamānasya kāmāḥ svāhā iti
1.6.2	yan me skannaṃ yad asmṛti iti ca skannāsmṛtihomau
1.6.3	yad adya tvā prayati iti saṃsthitahomāḥ
1.6.4	manasas pate iti uttamaṃ caturgṛhītena
1.6.5	barhir ājyaśeṣe 'nakti
1.6.6	pṛthivyai tvā iti mūlam antarikṣāya tvā iti madhyaṃ dive tvā iti agram evaṃ triḥ
1.6.7	saṃ barhir aktam ity anupraharati yathādevatam
1.6.8	sruvam agnau dhārayati
1.6.9	yad ājyadhānyāṃ tat saṃsrāvayati saṃsrāvabhāgās taviṣā bṛhantaḥ prastareṣṭhā barhiṣadaś ca devāḥ imaṃ yajñam abhi viśve gṛṇantaḥ svāhā devā amṛtā mādayantām iti
1.6.10	sruvo 'si ghṛtād aniśitaḥ sapatnakṣayaṇo divi ṣīda antarikṣe sīda pṛthivyāṃ sīdottaro 'haṃ bhūyāsam adhare matsapatnāḥ iti sruvaṃ prāgdaṇḍaṃ nidadhāti
1.6.11	vi muñcāmi brahmaṇā jātavedasam agniṃ hotāram ajaraṃ rathaspṛtam sarvā devānāṃ janimāni vidvān yathābhāgaṃ vahatu havyam agniḥ agnaye svāhā iti samidham ādadhāti
1.6.12	edho 'si iti dvitīyāṃ samid asi iti tṛtīyam
1.6.13	tejo 'si iti mukhaṃ vimārṣṭi
1.6.14	dakṣiṇenāgniṃ trīn viṣṇukramān kramate viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si iti dakṣiṇena pādenānusaṃharati savyam
1.6.15	sūryasyāvṛtam ity abhidakṣiṇam āvartate
1.6.16	aganma svaḥ ity ādityam īkṣate
1.6.17	indrasya vacasā vayaṃ mitrasya varuṇasya ca brahmaṇā sthāpitaṃ pātraṃ punar utthāpayāmasi ity apareṇāgnim udapātraṃ parihṛtyottareṇāgnim āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuvaḥ iti mārjayitvā barhiṣi patnyāñjalau ninayati samudraṃ vaḥ pra hiṇomi iti idaṃ janāsaḥ iti vā
1.6.18	vīrapatny ahaṃ bhūyāsam iti mukhaṃ vimārṣṭi
1.6.19	vratāni vratapataye iti samidham ādadhāti
1.6.20	satyaṃ tvartena iti pariṣicyodañci havirucchiṣṭāny udvāsayati
1.6.21	pūrṇapātraṃ dakṣiṇā
1.6.22	nādakṣiṇaṃ haviḥ kurvīta yaḥ kurute kṛtyām ātmanaḥ kurute iti brāhmaṇam
1.6.23	anvāhāryaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayati
1.6.24	yad vai yajñasyānanvitaṃ bhavati tad anvāhāryeṇānvāhriyate
1.6.25	etad anvāhāryasyānvāhāryatvam
1.6.26	īḍyā vā anye devāḥ saparyeṇyā anye devā īḍyā devā brāhmaṇāḥ saparyeṇyāḥ
1.6.27	yajñenaiveḍyān prīṇāti anvāhāryeṇa saparyeṇyān
1.6.28	te 'syobhe prītā yajñe bhavantīti
1.6.29	imau darśapūrṇamāsau vyākhyātau
1.6.30	darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ pākayajñāḥ
1.6.31	kumbhīpākād eva vyuddhāraṃ juhuyāt
1.6.32	adhiśrayaṇaparyagnikaraṇābhighāraṇodvāsanālaṃkaraṇotpavanaiḥ saṃskṛtya
1.6.33	athāpi ślokau bhavataḥ ājyabhāgāntaṃ prāktantram ūrdhvaṃ sviṣṭakṛtā saha havīṃṣi yajña āvāpo yathā tantrasya tantavaḥ pākayajñān samāsādyaikājyān ekabarhiṣaḥ ekasviṣṭakṛtaḥ kuryānnānāpi sati daivata iti
1.6.34	etenaivāmāvāsyo vyākhyātaḥ
1.6.35	aindrāgno 'tra dvitīyo bhavati
1.6.36	tayor vyatikrame tvam agne vratapā asi kāmas tadagre iti śāntāḥ
1.7.1	aśnātyanādeśe sthālīpākaḥ
1.7.2	puṣṭikarmasu sārūpavatse
1.7.3	ājyaṃ juhoti
1.7.4	samidham ādadhāti
1.7.5	āvapati vrīhiyavatilān
1.7.6	bhakṣayati kṣīraudanapuroḍāśarasān
1.7.7	manthaudanau prayacchati
1.7.8	pūrvaṃ triṣaptīyam
1.7.9	udakacodanāyām udapātraṃ pratīyāt

4.11.7	khe lūnāṃśca palāśatsarūn nivṛtte nighṛṣyādhāya śiśne grāmaṃ praviśati
4.11.8	śamīm aśvattha iti mantrokte 'gniṃ mathitvā puṃsyāḥ sarpiṣi paidvam iva
4.11.9	madhumanthe pāyayati
4.11.10	kṛṣṇorṇābhiḥ pariveṣṭya badhnāti
4.11.11	yantāsīti mantroktaṃ badhnāti
4.11.12	ṛdhaṅmantra ity ekā yatheyaṃ pṛthivy acyuteti garbhadṛṃhaṇāni
4.11.13	jambhagṛhītāya prathamāvarjaṃ jyāṃ trir udgrathya badhnāti
4.11.14	loṣṭān anvṛcaṃ prāśayati
4.11.15	śyāmasikatābhiḥ śayanaṃ parikirati
4.11.16	yām icched vīraṃ janayed iti dhātṛvyābhir udaram abhimantrayate
4.11.17	prajāpatir iti prajākāmāyā upasthe juhoti
4.11.18	lohitājāpiśitānyāśayati
4.11.19	prapāntāni
4.11.20	yau te māteti mantroktau badhnāti
4.11.21	yathedaṃ bhūmyā adhi yathā vṛkṣaṃ vāñcha me yathāyaṃ vāha iti saṃspṛṣṭayor vṛkṣalibujayoḥ śakalāvantareṣusthakarāñjanakuṣṭhamadughareṣmamathitatṛṇam ājyena saṃnīya saṃspṛśati
4.11.22	uttudas tvety aṅgulyopanudati

4.12.1	sahasraśṛṅga iti svāpanam
4.12.2	udapātreṇa saṃpātavatā śālāṃ saṃprokṣyāparasmin dvārapakṣe nyubjati

4.12.4	ulūkhalam uttarāṃ sraktiṃ dakṣiṇaśayanapādaṃ tantūn abhimantrayate
4.12.5	asthād dyaur iti niveṣṭanam
4.12.6	āveṣṭanena vaṃśāgram avabadhya madhyamāyāṃ badhnāti
4.12.7	śayanapādam utpale ca
4.12.8	ākṛṣṭe ca
4.12.9	ākarṣeṇa tilāñjuhoti
4.12.10	idaṃ yat preṇya iti śiraḥkarṇam abhimantrayate
4.12.11	keśān dhārayati
4.12.12	bhagena mā nyastikedaṃ khanāmīti sauvarcalam oṣadhivacchuklaprasūnaṃ śirasyupacṛtya grāmaṃ praviśati
4.12.13	rathajitām iti māṣasmarān nivapati
4.12.14	śarabhṛṣṭīr ādīptāḥ pratidiśam abhyasyatyarvācyā āvalekhanyāḥ
4.12.15	bhagam asyā varca iti mālāniṣpramandadantadhāvanakeśam īśānahatāyā anustaraṇyā vā kośam ulūkhaladaraṇe triśile nikhanati
4.12.16	mālām upamathyānvāha
4.12.17	trīṇi keśamaṇḍalāni kṛṣṇasūtrena vigrathya triśile 'śmottarāṇi vyatyāsam
4.12.18	athāsyai bhagam utkhanati yaṃ te bhagaṃ nicakhnus triśile yaṃ catuḥśile idaṃ tam utkhanāmi prajayā ca dhanena ceti
4.12.19	imāṃ khanāmīti bāṇāparṇīṃ lohitājāyā drapsena saṃnīya śayanam anuparikirati
4.12.20	abhi te 'dhām ity adhastāt palāśam upacṛtati
4.12.21	upa te 'dhām ity uparyupāsyati
4.12.22	kāmaṃ vineṣyamāṇo 'pāghenāsaṃkhyātāḥ śarkarāḥ parikiran vrajati
4.12.23	saṃmṛdnañjapati
4.12.24	asaṃmṛdnan
4.12.25	īrṣyāyā dhrājiṃ janād viśvajanīnāt tvāṣṭreṇāham iti pratijāpaḥ pradānābhimarśanāni
4.12.26	prathamena vakṣaṇāsu mantroktam
4.12.27	agner iveti paraśuphāṇṭam
4.12.28	ava jyām iveti dṛṣṭvāśmānam ādatte
4.12.29	dvitīyayābhinidadhāti
4.12.30	tṛtīyayābhiniṣṭhīvati
4.12.31	chāyāyāṃ sajyaṃ karoti
4.12.32	ayaṃ darbha ity oṣadhivat
4.12.33	agne jātān iti na vīraṃ janayet prānyān iti na vijāyetety aśvatarīmūtram aśmamaṇḍalābhyāṃ saṃghṛṣya bhakte 'laṃkāre
4.12.34	sīmantam anvīkṣate
4.12.35	api vṛśceti jāyāyai jāram anvāha
4.12.36	klībapade bādhakaṃ dhanur vṛścati

5.8.12	darbhābhyām anvārabhate
5.8.13	paścād uttarato 'gneḥ pratyakśīrṣīm udakpādīṃ nividhyati
5.8.14	sam asyai tanvā bhavety anyataraṃ darbham avāsyati
5.8.15	atha prāṇān āsthāpayati prajānanta iti
5.8.16	dakṣiṇatas tiṣṭhan rakṣohaṇaṃ japati
5.8.17	saṃjñaptāyāṃ juhoti / yad vaśā māyum akratoro vā paḍbhir āhata / agnir mā tasmād enaso viśvān muñcatv aṃhasa iti
5.8.18	udapātreṇa patnyabhivrajya mukhādīni gātrāṇi prakṣālayate
5.8.19	mukhaṃ śundhasva devayajyāyā iti
5.8.20	prāṇān iti nāsike
5.8.21	cakṣur iti cakṣuṣī
5.8.22	śrotram iti karṇau
5.8.23	yat te krūraṃ yad āsthitam iti samantaṃ rajjudhānam
5.8.24	caritrāṇīti pādān samāhṛtya
5.8.25	nābhim iti nābhim
5.8.26	meḍhram iti meḍhram
5.8.27	pāyum iti pāyum
5.8.28	yat te krūraṃ yad āsthitaṃ tacchundhasveti avaśiṣṭāḥ pārśvadeśe 'vasicya yathārthaṃ vrajati

5.8.31	idam aham āmuṣyāyaṇasyāmuṣyāḥ putrasya prāṇāpānāv apakṛntāmīty apakṛtya
5.8.32	adharapravraskena lohitasyāpahatya
5.8.33	idam aham āmuṣyāyaṇasyāmuṣyāḥ putrasya prāṇāpānau nikhanāmīty āsye nikhanati

5.9.1	yadyaṣṭāpadī syād garbhamañjalau sahiraṇyaṃ sayavaṃ vā ya ātmadā iti khadāyāṃ tryaratnāvagnau sakṛjjuhoti

5.10.53	prehi prahareti kāpiñjalāni svastyayanāni bhavanti
5.10.54	prehi prahara vā dāvān gṛhebhyaḥ svastaye / kapiñjala pradakṣiṇaṃ śatapattrābhi no vada / bhadraṃ vada dakṣiṇato bhadram uttarato vada / bhadraṃ purastān no vada bhadraṃ paścāt kapiñjala / śunaṃ vada dakṣiṇataḥ śunam uttarato vada / śunaṃ purastān no vada śunaṃ paścāt kapiñjala / bhadraṃ vada putrair bhadraṃ vada gṛheṣu ca / bhadram asmākaṃ vada bhadraṃ no abhayaṃ vada / āvadaṃstvaṃ śakune bhadram āvada tūṣṇīm āsīnaḥ sumatiṃ cikiddhi naḥ / yad utpatan vadasi karkarir yathā bṛhad vadema vidathe suvīrāḥ / yauvanāni mahayasi jigyuṣām iva dundubhiḥ / kapiñjala pradakṣiṇaṃ śatapattrābhi no vada / iti kāpiñjalāni svastyayanāni bhavanti

6.3.1	sapatnahanam ity ṛṣabhaṃ saṃpātavantam atisṛjati
6.3.2	āśvatthīr avapannāḥ
6.3.3	svayam indrasyauja iti prakṣālayati
6.3.4	jiṣṇave yogāyety apo yunakti
6.3.5	vātasya raṃhitasyāmṛtasya yonir iti pratigṛhṇāti
6.3.6	uttamāḥ pratāpyādharāḥ pradāyainam enān adharācaḥ parāco 'vācas tapasas tam unnayata devāḥ pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ prajāpatiḥ prathamo devatānām ity atisṛjati
6.3.7	idam ahaṃ yo mā prācyā diśo 'ghāyur abhidāsād apavādīd iṣugūhas tasyemau prāṇāpānāvapakrāmāmi brahmaṇā
6.3.8	dakṣiṇāyāḥ pratīcyā udīcyā dhruvāyā vyadhvāyā ūrdhvāyāḥ

6.3.10	evam abhiṣṭhānāpohananiveṣṭanāni

6.3.12	brāhmaṇād vajram udyacchamānācchaṅkante māṃ haniṣyasi māṃ haniṣyasīti tebhyo 'bhayaṃ vadeccham agnaye śaṃ pṛthivyai śam antarikṣāya śaṃ vāyave śaṃ dive śaṃ sūryāya śaṃ candrāya śaṃ nakṣatrebhyaḥ śaṃ gandharvāpsarobhyaḥ śaṃ sarpetarajanebhyaḥ śivam mahyam iti
6.3.13	yo va āpo 'pāṃ yaṃ vayam apām asmai vajram ity anvṛcam udavajrān
6.3.14	viṣṇoḥ kramo 'sīti viṣṇukramān

6.3.27	nir durarmaṇya iti saṃdhāvyābhimṛśati
7.1.1	svastidā ye te panthāna ity adhvānaṃ dakṣiṇena prakrāmati
7.1.2	vyudasyatyasaṃkhyātāḥ śarkarāḥ
7.1.3	tṛṇāni chittvopatiṣṭhate
7.1.4	āre amūḥ pāre pātaṃ na ya enaṃ pariṣīdanti yad āyudhaṃ daṇḍena vyākhyātam
7.1.5	diṣṭyā mukhaṃ vimāya saṃviśati
7.1.6	trīṇi padāni pramāyottiṣṭhati
7.1.7	tisro diṣṭīḥ
7.1.8	pretaṃ pādāv ity avasasya
7.1.9	pāyayati
7.1.10	upasthās ta iti trīṇyopyātikrāmati
7.1.11	svasti mātra iti niśyupatiṣṭhate
7.1.12	indram ahaṃ iti paṇyaṃ saṃpātavad utthāpayati
7.1.13	nimṛjya digyuktābhyāṃ doṣo gāya pātaṃ na iti pañcānaḍudbhyo yamo mṛtyur viśvajicchakadhūmaṃ bhavāśarvāv ity upadadhīta
7.1.14	uttamena sārūpavatsasya rudrāya trir juhoti
7.1.15	upottamena suhṛdo brāhmaṇasya śakṛtpiṇḍān parvasvādhāya śakadhūmaṃ kim adyāhar iti pṛcchati
7.1.16	bhadraṃ sumaṅgalam iti pratipadyate
7.1.17	yuktayor mā no devā yas te sarpa iti śayanaśālorvarāḥ parilikhati
7.1.18	tṛṇāni yugatardmanā saṃpātavanti dvāre pracṛtati
7.1.19	ūbadhyaṃ sambhinatti
7.1.20	nikhanati
7.1.21	ādadhāti
7.1.22	apāmārgaprasūnān kudrīcīśaphān parācīnamūlān
7.2.1	udita iti khādiraṃ śaṅkuṃ saṃpātavantam udgṛhṇan nikhanan gā anuvrajati
7.2.2	ninayanaṃ samuhya cāre sārūpavatsasyendrāya trir juhoti
7.2.3	diśyān balīn harati
7.2.4	pratidiśam upatiṣṭhate
7.2.5	madhye pañcamam anirdiṣṭam
7.2.6	śeṣaṃ ninayati
7.2.7	brahma jajñānaṃ bhavāśarvāv ityāsannam araṇye parvataṃ yajate
7.2.8	anyasmin bhavaśarvapaśupatyugrarudramahādeveśānānāṃ pṛthag āhutīḥ
7.2.9	goṣṭhe ca dvitīyam aśnāti
7.2.10	darbhān ādhāya dhūpayati
7.2.11	bhūtyai vaḥ puṣṭyai va iti prathamajayor mithunayor mukham anakti
7.2.12	tisro naladaśākhā vatsān pāyayati
7.2.13	śākhayodakadhārayā gāḥ parikrāmati
7.2.14	aśmavarma ma iti ṣaḍ aśmanaḥ saṃpātavataḥ sraktiṣūparyadhastān nikhanati
7.2.15	alasālā ity ālabheṣajam
7.2.16	trīṇi silāñjālāgrāṇyurvarāmadhye nikhanati
7.2.17	hataṃ tardaṃ iti ayasā sīsaṃ karṣann urvarāṃ parikrāmati
7.2.18	aśmano 'vakirati
7.2.19	tardam avaśirasaṃ vadanāt keśena samuhyorvarāmadhye nikhanati
7.2.20	uktaṃ cāre
7.2.21	balīn haratyāśāyā āśāpataye 'śvibhyāṃ kṣetrapataye
7.2.22	yadaitebhyaḥ kurvīta vāgyatas tiṣṭhed āstamayāt
7.3.1	ye panthāna iti parītyopadadhīta
7.3.2	prayacchati
7.3.3	yasyās te yat te devī viṣāṇā pāśān ity unmocanapratirūpaṃ saṃpātavantaṃ karoti
7.3.4	vācā baddhāya bhūmiparilekham
7.3.5	āyana iti śamanam antarā hradaṃ karoti
7.3.6	śāle ca
7.3.7	avakayā śālāṃ paritanoti
7.3.8	śapyamānāya prayacchati
7.3.9	nidagdhaṃ prakṣālayati
7.3.10	mahīm ū ṣv iti taraṇānyālambhayati
7.3.11	dūrānnāvaṃ saṃpātavatīṃ naumaṇiṃ badhnāti
7.3.12	prapatha iti naṣṭaiṣiṇāṃ prakṣālitābhyaktapāṇipādānāṃ dakṣiṇān pāṇīn nimṛjyotthāpayati
7.3.13	evaṃ saṃpātavataḥ
7.3.14	nimṛjyaikaviṃśatiṃ śarkarāścatuṣpathe 'vakṣipyāvakirati
7.3.15	namaskṛtyeti mantroktam
7.3.16	aṃholiṅgānām āpo bhojanahavīṃṣyabhimarśanopasthānam ādityasya
7.3.17	svayaṃ haviṣāṃ bhojanam
7.3.18	viśve devā ity āyuṣyāṇi
7.3.19	sthālīpāke ghṛtapiṇḍān pratinīyāśnāti
7.3.20	asmin vasu yad ābadhnan nava prāṇān iti yugmakṛṣṇalam ādiṣṭānāṃ sthālīpāka ādhāya badhnāti
7.3.21	āśayati
7.4.1	āyurdā iti godānaṃ kārayiṣyan saṃbhārān saṃbharati
7.4.2	amamrim ojomānīṃ dūrvām akarṇam aśmamaṇḍalam ānaḍuhaśakṛtpiṇḍaṃ ṣaḍ darbhaprāntāni kaṃsam ahate vasane śuddham ājyam śāntā oṣadhīr navam udakumbham
7.4.3	bāhyataḥ śāntavṛkṣasyedhmaṃ prāñcam upasamādhāya
7.4.4	parisamuhya paryukṣya paristīrya barhir udapātram upasādya paricaraṇenājyaṃ paricarya
7.4.5	nityān purastāddhomān hutvājyabhāgau ca
7.4.6	paścād agneḥ prāṅmukha upaviśyānvārabdhāya śāntyudakaṃ karoti
7.4.7	tatraitat sūktam anuyojayati
7.4.8	trir evāgniṃ samprokṣati triḥ paryukṣati
7.4.9	triḥ kārayamāṇam ācāmayati ca samprokṣati ca
7.4.10	śakṛtpiṇḍasya sthālarūpaṃ kṛtvā suhṛde brāhmaṇāya prayacchati
7.4.11	tat suhṛd dakṣiṇato 'gner udaṅmukha āsīno dhārayati
7.4.12	athāsmā anvārabdhāya karoti
7.4.13	āyurdā ity anena sūktenājyaṃ juhvan mūrdhni saṃpātān ānayati
7.4.14	dakṣiṇe pāṇāvaśmamaṇḍala udapātra uttarasaṃpātān sthālarūpa ānayati
7.4.15	amamrim ojomānīṃ codapātre 'vadhāya
7.4.16	sthālarūpe dūrvāṃ śāntyudakam uṣṇodakaṃ caikadhābhisamāsicya
7.4.17	āyam agan savitā kṣureṇa ity udapātram anumantrayate
7.4.18	aditiḥ śmaśru ity undati
7.4.19	yat kṣureṇa ity udakpattraṃ kṣuram adbhi ścotya triḥ pramārṣṭi
7.4.20	yenāvapat iti dakṣiṇasya keśapakṣasya darbhapiñjūlyā keśān abhinidhāya pracchidya sthālarūpe karoti
7.4.21	evam eva dvitīyaṃ karoti
7.4.22	evaṃ tṛtīyam
7.4.23	evam evottarasya keśapakṣasya karoti
7.5.1	atha nāpitaṃ samādiśatyakṣaṇvan vapa keśaśmaśrur oma parivapa nakhāni kurviti
7.5.2	punaḥ prāṇaḥ punar maitv indriyam iti trir nimṛjya
7.5.3	tvayi mahimānaṃ sādayāmīty antato yojayet
7.5.4	athainam uptakeśaśmaśruṃ kṛttanakham āplāvayati
7.5.5	hiraṇyavarṇā ity etena sūktena gandhapravādābhir alaṃkṛtya
7.5.6	svaktaṃ ma ity ānakti
7.5.7	athainam ahatena vasanena paridhāpayati paridhatteti dvābhyām
7.5.8	ehy aśmānam ātiṣṭheti dakṣiṇena pādenāśmamaṇḍalam āsthāpya pradakṣiṇam agnim anupariṇīya
7.5.9	athāsya vāso nirmuṣṇāti yasya te vāsa ity anayā
7.5.10	athainam apareṇāhatena vasanenācchādayaty ayaṃ vaste garbhaṃ pṛthivyā iti pañcabhiḥ
7.5.11	yathā dyaur manase cetase dhiya iti mahāvrīhīṇāṃ sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvā śāntyudakenopasicyābhimantrya prāśayati
7.5.12	prāṇāpānāv ojo 'sīty upadadhīta
7.5.13	tubhyam eva jarimanniti kumāraṃ mātāpitarau triḥ samprayacchete
7.5.14	ghṛtapiṇḍān āśayataḥ
7.5.15	cūḍākaraṇam ca godānena vyākhyātam
7.5.16	paridhāpanāśmamaṇḍalavarjam
7.5.17	śive te stām iti paridānāntāni
7.5.18	pārthivasya mā pra gāmeti catasraḥ sarvāṇyapiyanti
7.5.19	amamrim ojomānīṃ ca dūrvāṃ ca keśāṃśca śakṛtpiṇḍaṃ caikadhābhisamāhṛtya
7.5.20	śāntavṛkṣasyoparyādadhāti
7.5.21	adhikaraṇaṃ brahmaṇaḥ kaṃsavasanaṃ gaur dakṣiṇā
7.5.22	brāhmaṇān bhaktenopepsanti
7.6.1	upanayanam
7.6.2	āyam aganniti mantroktam
7.6.3	yat kṣureṇety uktam
7.6.4	yenāvapad iti śakṛd apiñjūli
7.6.5	laukikaṃ ca samānām ā paridhānāt
7.6.6	upetapūrvasya niyataṃ savān dāsyato 'gnīn ādhāsyamānaparyavetavratadīkṣiṣyamāṇānām
7.6.7	soṣṇodakaṃ śāntyudakaṃ pradakṣiṇam anupariṇīya purastād agneḥ pratyaṅmukham avasthāpya
7.6.8	āha brūhi
7.6.9	brahmacaryam āgam upa mā nayasveti
7.6.10	ko nāmāsi kiṃgotra ity asāviti yathā nāmagotre bhavatas tathā prabrūhi
7.6.11	ārṣeyaṃ mā kṛtvā bandhumantam upanaya
7.6.12	ārṣeyaṃ tvā kṛtvā bandhumantam upanayāmīti
7.6.13	oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar janad om ity añjalāvudakam āsiñcati
7.6.14	uttaro 'sāni brahmacāribhya ity uttamaṃ pāṇim anvādadhāti
7.6.15	eṣa ma ādityaputras tan me gopāyasvety ādityena samīkṣate
7.6.16	apakrāman pauruṣeyād vṛṇāna ity enaṃ bāhugṛhītaṃ prāñcam avasthāpya dakṣiṇena pāṇinā nābhideśe 'bhisaṃstabhya japati
7.6.17	asmin vasu vasavo dhārayantu viśve devā vasava āyātu mitro 'mutrabhūyād antakāya mṛtyava ārabhasva prāṇāya namo viṣāsahim ity abhimantrayate
7.6.18	athāpi paritvaramāṇa āyātu mitra ity api khalv etāvataivopanīto bhavati
7.6.19	pracchādya trīn prāṇāyāmān kṛtvāvacchādya vatsatarīm udapātre samavekṣayet
7.6.20	sam indra naḥ saṃ varcaseti dvābhyām utsṛjanti gām
7.7.1	śraddhāyā duhiteti dvābhyāṃ bhādramauñjīṃ mekhalāṃ badhnāti
7.7.2	mitrāvaruṇayos tvā hastābhyāṃ prasūtaḥ praśiṣā prayacchāmīti pālāśaṃ daṇḍaṃ prayacchati
7.7.3	mitrāvaruṇayos tvā hastābhyāṃ prasūtaḥ praśiṣā pratigṛhṇāmi / suśravaḥ suśravasaṃ mā kurv avakro 'vithuro 'haṃ bhūyāsam iti pratigṛhṇāti
7.7.4	śyeno 'sīti ca
7.7.5	athainaṃ vratādānīyāḥ samidha ādhāpayati
7.7.6	agne vratapate vrataṃ cariṣyāmi tac chakeyaṃ tat samāpeyaṃ tan me rādhyatāṃ tan me samṛdhyatāṃ tan me mā vyanaśat tena rādhyāsaṃ tat te prabravīmi tad upākaromi agnaye vratapataye svāhā
7.7.7	vāyo vratapate / sūrya vratapate / candra vratapate / āpo vratapatnyaḥ / devā vratapatayaḥ / vratānāṃ vratapatayo vratam acāriṣaṃ tad aśakaṃ tat samāptaṃ tan me rāddhaṃ tan me samṛddhaṃ tan me mā vyanaśat tena rādho 'smi tad vaḥ prabravīmi tad upākaromi vratebhyo vratapatibhyaḥ svāheti
7.7.8	athainaṃ baddhamekhalam āhitasamitkaṃ sāvitrīṃ vācayati
7.7.9	pacchaḥ prathamam
7.7.10	tato 'rdharcaśaḥ
7.7.11	tataḥ saṃhitām
7.7.12	athainaṃ saṃśāsty agneś cāsi brahmacārin mama cāpo 'śāna karma kurūrdhvas tiṣṭhan mā divā svāpsīḥ samidha ādhehi
7.7.13	athainaṃ bhūtebhyaḥ paridadāty agnaye tvā paridadāmi brahmaṇe tvā paridadāmy udaṅkyāya tvā śūlvāṇāya paridadāmi śatruṃjayāya tvā kṣātrāṇāya paridadāmi mārtyuṃjayāya tvā mārtyavāya paridadāmy aghorāya tvā paridadāmi takṣakāya tvā vaiśāleyāya paridadāmi hāhāhūhūbhyāṃ tvā gandharvābhyāṃ paridadāmi yogakṣemābhyāṃ tvā paridadāmi bhayāya ca tvābhayāya ca paridadāmi viśvebhyas tvā devebhyaḥ paridadāmi sarvebhyas tvā devebhyaḥ paridadāmi viśvebhyas tvā bhūtebhyaḥ paridadāmi sarvebhyas tvā bhūtebhyaḥ paridadāmi saprajāpatikebhyaḥ
7.7.14	svasti caratād iheti mayi ramantāṃ brahmacāriṇa ity anugṛhṇīyāt
7.7.15	nānupraṇudet
7.7.16	praṇītīr abhyāvartasvety abhyātmam āvartayati
7.7.17	yathāpaḥ pravatā yanti yathā māsā aharjaram / evā mā brahmacāriṇo dhātar āyantu sarvadā / svāhety ācāryaḥ samidham ādadhāti
7.8.1	śraddhāyā duhiteti dvābhyāṃ bhādramauñjīṃ mekhalāṃ brāhmaṇāya badhnāti
7.8.2	maurvīṃ kṣatriyāya dhanurjyāṃ vā
7.8.3	kṣaumikīṃ vaiśyāya
7.8.4	mitrāvaruṇayos tvā hastābhyāṃ prasūtaḥ praśiṣā prayacchāmīti pālāśaṃ daṇḍaṃ brāhmaṇāya prayacchati
7.8.5	āśvatthaṃ kṣatriyāya
7.8.6	nyagrodhāvarohaṃ vaiśyāya
7.8.7	yadyasya daṇḍo bhajyeta ya ṛte cid abhiśriṣa ity etayālabhyābhimantrayate
7.8.8	sarvatra śīrṇe bhinne naṣṭe 'nyaṃ kṛtvā punar maitv indriyam ity ādadhīta
7.8.9	atha vāsāṃsi
7.8.10	aiṇeyahāriṇāni brāhmaṇasya
7.8.11	rauravapārṣatāni kṣatriyasya
7.8.12	ājāvikāni vaiśyasya
7.8.13	sarveṣāṃ kṣaumaśāṇakambalavastram
7.8.14	kāṣāyāṇi
7.8.15	vastraṃ cāpyakāṣāyam
7.8.16	bhavati bhikṣāṃ dehīti brāhmaṇaś caret
7.8.17	bhikṣāṃ bhavatī dadātv iti kṣatriyaḥ
7.8.18	dehi bhikṣāṃ bhavatīti vaiśyaḥ
7.8.19	sapta kulāni brāhmaṇaś caret trīṇi kṣatriyo dve vaiśyaḥ
7.8.20	sarvaṃ grāmaṃ cared bhaikṣaṃ stenapatitavarjam
7.8.21	mayy agra iti pañcapraśnena juhoti
7.8.22	saṃ mā siñcantv iti triḥ paryukṣati
7.8.23	yad agne tapasā tapo 'gne tapas tapyāmaha iti dvābhyāṃ parisamūhayati
7.8.24	idam āpaḥ pravahateti pāṇī prakṣālayate
7.8.25	saṃ mā siñcantv iti triḥ paryukṣati
7.8.26	agne samidham āhārṣam ity ādadhāti catasraḥ
7.8.27	edho 'sīty ūṣmabhakṣaṃ bhakṣayaty ā nidhanāt
7.8.28	tvaṃ no medha ity upatiṣṭhate
7.8.29	yad annam iti tisṛbhir bhaikṣasya juhoti
7.8.30	aharahaḥ samidha āhṛtyaivaṃ sāyaṃ prātar abhyādadhyāt
7.8.31	medhājanana āyuṣyair juhuyāt
7.8.32	yathākāmaṃ dvādaśarātram arasāśī bhavati
7.9.1	bhadrāya karṇaḥ krośatu bhadrāyākṣi vi vepatām / parā duḥṣvapnyaṃ suva yad bhadraṃ tan na ā suva / akṣivepaṃ duḥṣvapnyam ārtiṃ puruṣareṣiṇīm / tad asmad aśvinā yuvam apriye prati muñcatam / yat pārśvād uraso me aṅgādaṅgād avavepate / aśvinā puṣkarasrajā tasmān naḥ pātam aṃhasa iti karṇaṃ krośantam anumantrayate
7.9.2	akṣi vā sphurat
7.9.3	vi devā jarasota devā āvatas ta upa priyam antakāya mṛtyava ā rabhasva prāṇāya namo viṣāsahim ity abhimantrayate
7.9.4	brāhmaṇoktam ṛṣihastaś ca
7.9.5	karmaṇe vāṃ veṣāya vāṃ sukṛtāya vām iti pāṇī prakṣālya
7.9.6	nir durarmaṇya iti saṃdhāvya
7.9.7	śuddhā na āpa iti niṣṭhīvya jīvābhir ācamya
7.9.8	ehi jīvam ity āñjanamaṇiṃ badhnāti
7.9.9	vātāj jāta iti kṛśanam
7.9.10	nava prāṇān iti mantroktam
7.9.11	ghṛtād ulluptam ā tvā cṛtatv ṛtubhiṣ ṭvā muñcāmi tvota devā āvatas ta upa priyam antakāya mṛtyava ā rabhasva prāṇāya namo viṣāsahim ity abhimantrayate
7.9.12	nir durarmaṇya iti sarvasurabhicūrṇair araṇye 'pratīhāraṃ pralimpati
7.9.13	atha nāmakaraṇam
7.9.14	ā rabhasvemām ity avichinnām udakadhārām ālambhayati

7.9.19	śivau te stām iti vrīhiyavau prāśayati
7.9.20	ahne ca tvety ahorātrābhyāṃ paridadāti
7.9.21	śarade tvety ṛtubhyaḥ
7.9.22	ud asya ketavo mūrdhāhaṃ viṣāsahiṃ ity udyantam upatiṣṭhate
7.9.23	madhyaṃdine 'staṃ yantaṃ sakṛt paryāyābhyām
7.9.24	aṃholiṅgānām āpo bhojanahavīṃṣyuktāni
7.9.25	uttamāsu yan mātalī rathakrītam iti sarvāsāṃ dvitīyā

7.10.2	upatiṣṭhate
7.10.3	idaṃ janāsa iti dyāvāpṛthivyai puṣṭikāmaḥ
7.10.4	saṃpatkāmaḥ
7.10.5	indra juṣasva itīndraṃ balakāmaḥ
7.10.6	indram ahaṃ iti paṇyakāmaḥ
7.10.7	ud enam uttaraṃ naya yo 'smān indraḥ sutrāmā iti grāmakāmaḥ
7.10.8	grāmasāṃpadānām apyayaḥ
7.10.9	yaśasaṃ mendra iti yaśaskāmaḥ
7.10.10	mahyam āpa iti vyacaskāmaḥ
7.10.11	āgacchata iti jāyākāmaḥ
7.10.12	vṛṣendrasya iti vṛṣakāmaḥ
7.10.13	ā tvāhārṣam dhruvā dyaur iti dhrauvyakāmaḥ
7.10.14	tyam ū ṣu trātāram ā mandrair iti svastyayanakāmaḥ

7.10.16	pṛthivyām iti mantroktam
7.10.17	tad id āsa dhītī vā itīndrāgnī
7.10.18	yasyedam ā rajo 'tharvāṇaṃ aditir dyaur diteḥ putrāṇām bṛhaspate savitar ity abhyuditaṃ brahmacāriṇaṃ bodhayati
7.10.19	dhātā dadhātu prajāpatir janayati anv adya no yan na indro yayor ojasā viṣṇor nu kaṃ agnāviṣṇū somārudrā sinīvāli bṛhaspatir naḥ yat te devā akṛṇvan pūrṇā paścāt prajāpate abhyarcata ko asyā na iti prajāpatim
7.10.20	agna indraś ca iti mantroktān sarvakāmaḥ
7.10.21	ya īśe ye bhakṣayanta itīndrāgnī lokakāmaḥ
7.10.22	annaṃ dadāti prathamam
7.10.23	paśūpākaraṇam uttamam
7.10.24	savapurastāddhomā yujyante
7.10.25	doṣo gāya ity atharvāṇaṃ samāvṛtyāśnāti
7.10.26	abhayaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī śyeno 'si iti pratidiśaṃ saptarṣīn abhayakāmaḥ
7.10.27	uttareṇa dīkṣitasya vā brahmacāriṇo vā daṇḍapradānaṃ
7.10.28	dyauś ca ma iti dyāvāpṛthivyai viriṣyati
7.10.29	yo agnāv iti rudrān svastyayanakāmaḥ svastyayanakāmaḥ
8.1.1	agnīn ādhāsyamānaḥ savān vā dāsyan saṃvatsaraṃ brāhmaudanikam agniṃ dīpayati

8.1.19	agne jāyasveti manthantāv anumantrayate
8.1.20	patnī mantraṃ saṃnamayati
8.1.21	yajamānaś ca
8.1.22	kṛṇuta dhūmam iti dhūmam
8.1.23	agne 'janiṣṭhā iti jātam
8.1.24	samiddho agna iti samidhyamānam
8.1.25	parehi nārīty udahṛtaṃ saṃpreṣyatyanuguptām alaṃkṛtām
8.1.26	emā agur ity āyatīm anumantrayate
8.1.27	uttiṣṭha nārīti patnīṃ saṃpreṣyati
8.1.28	prati kumbhaṃ gṛbhāyeti pratigṛhṇāti
8.1.29	ūrjo bhāga iti nidadhāti
8.1.30	iyaṃ mahīti carmāstṛṇāti prāggrīvam uttaraloma
8.1.31	pumān puṃsa iti carmārohayati
8.1.32	patnī hvayamānam
8.1.33	tṛtīyasyām apatyam anvāhvayati
8.1.34	ṛṣipraśiṣṭety udapātraṃ carmaṇi nidadhāti
8.1.35	tad āpas putrāsa iti sāpatyāv anunipadyete
8.2.1	prācīṃ prācīm iti mantroktam
8.2.2	catasṛbhir udapātram anupariyanti
8.2.3	pratidiśaṃ dhruveyaṃ virāḍ ity upatiṣṭhante
8.2.4	piteva putrān ity avarohya bhūmiṃ tenodakārthān kurvanti
8.2.5	pavitraiḥ samprokṣante
8.2.6	darbhāgrābhyāṃ carmahaviḥ samprokṣati
8.2.7	ādiṣṭānāṃ sānajānatyai prayacchati
8.2.8	tāṃs tredhā bhāga iti vrīhirāśiṣu nidadhāti
8.2.9	teṣāṃ yaḥ pitṝṇāṃ taṃ śrāddhaṃ karoti

8.2.11	yo devānāṃ tam agne sahasvān iti dakṣiṇaṃ jānv ācyāparājitābhimukhaḥ prahvo vā muṣṭiprasṛtāñjalibhiḥ kumbhyāṃ nirvapati
8.2.12	kumbhyā vā catuḥ

8.2.18	etau grāvāṇāv ayaṃ grāvety ulūkhalamusalaṃ śūrpaṃ prakṣālitaṃ carmaṇyādhāya
8.2.19	gṛhāṇa grāvāṇāv ity ubhayaṃ gṛhṇāti
8.2.20	sākaṃ sajātair iti vrīhīn ulūkhala āvapati
8.2.21	vanaspatir iti musalam ucchrayati
8.2.22	nirbhinddhy aṃśūn grāhiṃ pāpmānam ity avahanti
8.2.23	iyaṃ te dhītir varṣavṛddham iti śūrpaṃ gṛhṇāti
8.2.24	ūrdhvaṃ prajāṃ viśvavyacā ity udūhantīm
8.2.25	parā punīhi tuṣaṃ palāvān iti niṣpunatīm
8.2.26	pṛthag rūpāṇīty avakṣiṇatīm
8.2.27	trayo lokā ity avakṣīṇān abhimṛśataḥ
8.2.28	punar ā yantu śūrpam ity udvapati
8.2.29	upaśvasa ity apavevekti
8.2.30	pṛthivīṃ tvā pṛthivyām iti kumbhīm ālimpati
8.2.31	agne carur ity adhiśrayati
8.2.32	agniḥ pacann iti paryādadhāti
8.2.33	ṛṣipraśiṣṭety udakam apakarṣati
8.2.34	śuddhāḥ pūtāḥ pūtāḥ pavitrair iti pavitre antardhāya
8.2.35	udakam āsiñcati
8.2.36	brahmaṇā śuddhāḥ saṃkhyātā stokā ity āpas tāsu niktvā taṇḍulān āvapati
8.2.37	uruḥ prathasvodyodhantīti śrapayati
8.2.38	pra yaccha parśum iti darbhāhārāya dātraṃ prayacchati
8.2.39	oṣadhīr dāntu parvann ity upari parvaṇāṃ lunāti
8.2.40	navaṃ barhir iti barhi stṛṇāti
8.2.41	udehi vediṃ dhartā dhriyasvety udvāsayati
8.2.42	abhyāvartasveti kumbhīṃ pradakṣiṇam āvartayati
8.2.43	vanaspate stīrṇam iti barhiṣi pātrīṃ nidadhāti
8.2.44	aṃsadhrīm ity upadadhāti
8.2.45	upa stṛṇīhīty ājyenopastṛṇāti
8.2.46	upāstarīr ity upastīrṇām anumantrayate
8.3.1	aditer hastāṃ sarvān samāgā iti mantroktam
8.3.2	tata udakam ādāya pātryām ānayati
8.3.3	darvyā kumbhyām
8.3.4	darvikṛte tatraiva pratyānayati
8.3.5	darvyottamam apādāya tatsuhṛd dakṣiṇato 'gner udaṅmukha āsīno dhārayati
8.3.6	athoddharati
8.3.7	uddhṛte yad apādāya dhārayati tat uttarārdha ādadhāti
8.3.8	anuttarādharatāyā odanasya yad uttaraṃ tad uttaram odana evaudanaḥ
8.3.9	ṣaṣṭhyāṃ śaratsv iti paścād agner upasādayati
8.3.10	nidhiṃ nidhipā iti trīṇi kāṇḍāni karoti
8.3.11	yadyaj jāyeti mantroktam
8.3.12	sā patyāvanvārabhate
8.3.13	anvārabdheṣv ata ūrdhvaṃ karoti
8.3.14	agnī rakṣa iti paryagnikaroti
8.3.15	babhrer adhvaryo idam prāpam ity uparyāpānaṃ karoti
8.3.16	babhrer brahmann iti brūyād anadhvaryum
8.3.17	ghṛtena gātrā siñca sarpir iti sarpiṣā viṣyandayati
8.3.18	vasor yā dhārā ādityebhyo aṅgirobhya iti rasair upasiñcati
8.3.19	priyaṃ priyāṇām ity uttarato 'gner dhenvādīnyanumantrayate
8.3.20	tām atyāsarat prathameti yathoktaṃ dohayitvopasiñcati
8.3.21	atyāsarat prathamā dhokṣyamāṇā sarvān yajñān bibhratī vaiśvadevī / upa vatsaṃ sṛjata vāśyate gaur vy asṛṣṭa sumanā hiṃkṛṇoti / badhāna vatsam abhi dhehi bhuñjatī nijya godhug upa sīda dugdhi / irām asmā odanaṃ pinvamānā kīlālaṃ ghṛtaṃ madam annabhāgam / sā dhāvatu yamarājñaḥ savatsā sudughāṃ pathā prathameha dattā / atūrṇadattā prathamedam āgan vatsena gāṃ saṃ sṛja viśvarūpām iti
8.3.22	idaṃ me jyotiḥ sam agnaya iti hiraṇyam adhidadhāti

8.4.1	yad akṣeṣv iti samānavasanau bhavataḥ
8.4.2	dvitīyaṃ tat pāpacailaṃ bhavati tan manuṣyādhamāya dadyād ity eke
8.4.3	śṛtaṃ tvā havyam iti catura ārṣeyān bhṛgvaṅgirovid upasādayati
8.4.4	śuddhāḥ pūtā iti mantroktam
8.4.5	pakvaṃ kṣetrād varṣaṃ vanuṣvety apakarṣati
8.4.6	agnau tuṣān iti tuṣān āvapati
8.4.7	paraḥ kambūkān iti savyena pādena phalīkaraṇān apohati

8.4.11	arthaluptāni nivartante

8.4.18	athaitayor vibhāgaḥ
8.4.19	sūktena pūrvaṃ saṃpātavantaṃ karoti
8.4.20	śrāmyata itiprabhṛtibhir vā sūktenābhimantryābhinigadya dadyād dātā vācyamānaḥ
8.4.21	anuvākenottaraṃ saṃpātavantaṃ karoti

8.4.28	saṃpātavato 'bhimantryābhinigadya dadyād dātā vācyamānaḥ

8.5.1	āśānām iti catuḥśarāvam
8.5.2	yad rājāna ity avekṣati
8.5.3	padasnātasya pṛthakpādeṣvapūpān nidadhāti
8.5.4	nābhyāṃ pañcamam
8.5.5	unnahyan vasanena sahiraṇyaṃ saṃpātavantam
8.5.6	ā nayaitam ity aparājitād ajamānīyamānam anumantrayate
8.5.7	indrāya bhāgam iti agniṃ pariṇīyamānam

8.6.1	aghāyatām ity atra mukham apinahyamānam anumantrayate
8.6.2	sapatneṣu vajraṃ grāvā tvaiṣa iti nipatantam
8.6.3	vediṣ ṭa iti mantroktam āstṛṇāti
8.6.4	viṃśatyodanāsu śrayaṇīṣu śatam avadānāni vadhrīsaṃnaddhāni pṛthagodaneṣūpary ādadhati
8.6.5	madhyamāyāḥ prathame randhriṇy āmikṣāṃ daśame 'bhitaḥ sapta saptāpūpān pariśrayati
8.6.6	pañcadaśe puroḍāśau
8.6.7	agre hiraṇyam
8.6.8	apo devīr ity agrata udakumbhān
8.6.9	bālās ta iti sūktena saṃpātavatīm
8.6.10	pradakṣiṇam agnim anupariṇīyopaveśanaprakṣālanācamanam uktam

8.6.13	atha prāśnāti
8.6.14	agneṣ ṭvāsyena prāśnāmi bṛhaspater mukhena / indrasya tvā jaṭhare sādayāmi varuṇasyodare / tad yathā hutam iṣṭaṃ prāśnīyād devātmā tvā prāśnāmy ātmāsy ātmann ātmānaṃ me mā hiṃsīr iti prāśitam anumantrayate
8.6.15	yo 'gnir nṛmaṇā nāma brāhmaṇeṣu praviṣṭaḥ / tasmin ma eṣa suhuto 'stv odanaḥ sa mā mā hiṃsīt parame vyoman / so asmabhyam astu parame vyomann iti dātāraṃ vācayati

8.7.1	vāṅ ma āsann iti mantroktānyabhimantrayate
8.7.2	bṛhatā mano dyauś ca me punar maitv indriyam iti pratimantrayate
8.7.3	pratimantrite vyavadāyāśnanti
8.7.4	śataudanāyāṃ dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇāḥ
8.7.5	adhikaṃ dadataḥ kāmapraṃ sampadyate
8.7.6	brahmāsyety odane hradān pratidiśaṃ karoti
8.7.7	uparyāpānam
8.7.8	tadabhitaś catasro diśyāḥ kulyāḥ
8.7.9	tā rasaiḥ pūrayati
8.7.10	pṛthivyāṃ surayādbhir āṇḍīkādivanti mantroktāni pratidiśaṃ nidhāya
8.7.11	yam odanam ity atimṛtyum
8.7.12	anaḍvān ity anaḍvāham
8.7.13	sūryasya raśmīn iti karkīṃ sānūbandhyāṃ dadāti
8.7.14	āyaṃ gauḥ pṛśnir ayaṃ sahasram iti pṛśnim gām
8.7.15	devā imaṃ madhunā saṃyutaṃ yavaṃ iti paunaḥśilaṃ madhumantaṃ sahiraṇyaṃ saṃpātavantam
8.7.16	punantu mā devajanā iti pavitraṃ kṛśaram
8.7.17	kaḥ pṛśnim ity urvarām
8.7.18	sāhasra ity ṛṣabham
8.7.19	prajāpatiś cety anaḍvāham
8.7.20	namas te jāyamānāyai dadāmīti vaśām udapātreṇa saṃpātavatā samprokṣyābhimantryābhinigadya dadyād dātā vācyamānaḥ
8.7.21	bhūmiṣ ṭvety enāṃ pratigṛhṇāti

8.7.26	tad antar eva sūktena saṃpātavat karoti
8.7.27	udapātreṇa saṃpātavatā śālāṃ samprokṣyābhimantryābhinigadya dadyād dātā vācyamānaḥ
8.7.28	antarā dyāṃ ca pṛthivīṃ cety enāṃ pratigṛhṇāti
8.7.29	upamitām iti mantroktāni pracṛtati
8.7.30	mā naḥ pāśam ity abhimantrya dhārayati
8.7.31	nāsyāsthīnīti yathoktam

8.7.33	śataudanāṃ ca
8.8.1	saṃbhṛteṣu sāvikeṣu saṃbhāreṣu brāhmaṇam ṛtvijaṃ vṛṇīta
8.8.2	ṛṣim ārṣeyaṃ sudhātudakṣiṇam anaimittikam
8.8.3	eṣa ha vā ṛṣir ārṣeyaḥ sudhātudakṣiṇo yasya tryavarārdhyāḥ pūrvapuruṣā vidyācaraṇavṛttaśīlasampannāḥ
8.8.4	udagayana ity eke
8.8.5	athāta odanasavānām upācārakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
8.8.6	savān dattvāgnīn ādadhīta
8.8.7	sārvavaidika ity eke
8.8.8	sarve vedā dvikalpāḥ
8.8.9	māsaparārdhyā dīkṣā dvādaśarātro vā
8.8.10	trirātra ity eke
8.8.11	haviṣyabhakṣā syur brahmacāriṇaḥ
8.8.12	adhaḥ śayīran
8.8.13	kartṛdātārāv ā samāpanāt kāmaṃ na bhuñjīran saṃtatāś cet syuḥ
8.8.14	ahani samāptam ity eke
8.8.15	yātrārthaṃ dātārau vā dātā keśaśmaśruromanakhāni vāpayīta
8.8.16	keśavarjaṃ patnī
8.8.17	snātāvahatavasanau surabhiṇau vratavantau karmaṇyāv upavasataḥ
8.8.18	śvo bhūte yajñopavītī śāntyudakaṃ kṛtvā yajñavāstu ca samprokṣya brahmaudanikam agniṃ mathitvā
8.8.19	yad devā devaheḍanaṃ yad vidvāṃso yad avidvāṃso 'pamityam apratīttam ity etais tribhiḥ sūktair anvārabdhe dātari pūrṇahomaṃ juhuyāt
8.8.20	pūrvāhṇe bāhyataḥ śāntavṛkṣasyedhmaṃ prāñcam upasamādhāya
8.8.21	parisamuhya paryukṣya paristīrya barhir udapātram upasādya paricaraṇenājyaṃ paricarya
8.8.22	nityān purastāddhomān hutvājyabhāgau ca
8.8.23	paścād agneḥ palpūlitavihitam aukṣaṃ vānaḍuham vā rohitaṃ carma prāggrīvam uttaraloma paristīrya
8.8.24	pavitre kurute
8.8.25	darbhāv apracchinnaprāntau prakṣālyānulomam anumārṣṭi
8.8.26	dakṣiṇaṃ jānvācyāparājitābhimukhaḥ prahvo vā muṣṭinā prasṛtināñjalinā yasyāṃ śrapayiṣyan syāt tayā caturtham
8.8.27	śarāveṇa catuḥśarāvaṃ devasya tvā savituḥ prasava ṛṣibhyas tvārṣeyebhyas tvaikarṣaye tvā juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi
8.9.1	vasavas tvā gāyatreṇa chandasā nirvapantu / ūrjam akṣitam akṣīyamāṇam upajīvyāsam iti dātāraṃ vācayati
8.9.2	rudrās tvā traiṣṭubhena chandasā / ādityās tvā jāgatena chandasā / viśve tvā devā ānuṣṭubhena chandasā nirvapantu / ūrjam akṣitam akṣīyamāṇam upajīvyāsam iti dātāraṃ vācayati
8.9.3	niruptaṃ sūktenābhimṛśati
8.9.4	svargabrahmaudanau tantram
8.9.5	saṃnipāte brahmaudanamitam udakam āsecayed dvibhāgam
8.9.6	yāvantas taṇḍulāḥ syur nāvasiñcen na pratiṣiñcet
8.9.7	yadyavasiñcen mayi varco atho yaśa iti brahmā yajamānaṃ vācayati
8.9.8	atha pratiṣiñcet
8.9.9	ā pyāyasva saṃ te payāṃsīti dvābhyāṃ pratiṣiñcet
8.9.10	ā pyāyasva sam etu te viśvataḥ soma vṛṣṇyam / bhavā vājasya saṃgathe / saṃ te payāṃsi sam u yantu vājāḥ saṃ vṛṣṇyāny abhimātiṣāhaḥ / āpyāyamāno amṛtāya soma divi śravāṃsy uttamāni dhiṣveti
8.9.11	tatra ced upādhimātrāyāṃ nakhena na lavaṇasya kuryāt tenaivāsya tad vṛthānnaṃ sampadyate
8.9.12	ahataṃ vāso dakṣiṇata upaśete
8.9.13	tat sahiraṇyam
8.9.14	tatra dve udapātre nihite bhavataḥ
8.9.15	dakṣiṇam anyad antaram anyat
8.9.16	antaraṃ yato 'dhicariṣyan bhavati
8.9.17	bāhyaṃ jāṅmāyanam
8.9.18	tata udakam ādāya pātryām ānayati
8.9.19	darvyā kumbhyām
8.9.20	darvikṛte tatraiva pratyānayati
8.9.21	darvyottamam apādāya tatsuhṛd dakṣiṇato 'gner udaṅmukha āsīno dhārayati
8.9.22	athoddharati
8.9.23	uddhṛte yad apādāya dhārayati tad uttarārdha ādhāya rasair upasicya pratigrahītre dātopavahati
8.9.24	tasminn anvārabdhaṃ dātāraṃ vācayati
8.9.25	tantraṃ sūktaṃ pacchaḥ snātena yau te pakṣau yad atiṣṭhaḥ
8.9.26	yau te pakṣāv ajarau patatriṇau yābhyāṃ rakṣāṃsy apahaṃsy odana / tābhyāṃ pathyāsma sukṛtasya lokaṃ yatra ṛṣayaḥ prathamajāḥ purāṇāḥ / yad atiṣṭho divas pṛṣṭhe vyomann adhy odana / anvāyan satyadharmāṇo brāhmaṇā rādhasā saha
8.9.27	kramadhvam agninā nākaṃ pṛṣṭhāt pṛthivyā aham antarikṣam āruhaṃ svar yanto nāpekṣanta uruḥ prathasva mahatā mahimnedaṃ me jyotiḥ satyāya ceti tisraḥ sam agnaya iti sārdham etayā
8.9.28	ata ūrdhvaṃ vācite hute saṃsthite 'mūṃ te dadāmīti nāmagrāham upaspṛśet
8.9.29	sadakṣiṇaṃ kāmas tad ity uktam
8.9.30	ye bhakṣayanta iti purastāddhomāḥ
8.9.31	agne tvaṃ no antama uta trātā śivo bhavā varūthyaḥ / taṃ tvā śociṣṭha dīdivaḥ sumnāya nūnam īmahe sakhibhyaḥ / gayasphāno amīvahā vasuvit puṣṭivardhanaḥ / sumitraḥ sumano bhavety ājyabhāgau
8.9.32	pāṇāv udakam ānīyety uktam
8.9.33	pratimantraṇāntam
8.9.34	pratimantrite vyavadāyāśnanti
8.9.35	idāvatsarāyeti vratavisarjanam ājyaṃ juhuyāt
8.9.36	samidho 'bhyādadhyāt
8.9.37	tatra ślokau / yajuṣā mathite agnau yajuṣopasamāhite / savān dattvā savāgnes tu katham utsarjanaṃ bhavet / vācayitvā savān sarvān pratigṛhya yathāvidhi / hutvā saṃnatibhis tatrotsargaṃ kauśiko 'bravīt
8.9.38	prāñco 'parājitāṃ vā diśam avabhṛthāya vrajanti
8.9.39	apāṃ sūktair āplutya pradakṣiṇam āvṛtyāpa upaspṛśyānavekṣamāṇāḥ pratyudāvrajanti
8.9.40	brāhmaṇān bhaktenopepsanti
8.9.41	yathoktā dakṣiṇā yathoktā dakṣiṇā
9.1.1	pitryam agniṃ śamayiṣyañ jyeṣṭhasya cāvibhaktina ekāgnim ādhāsyan
9.1.2	amāvāsyāyāṃ pūrvasminn upaśāle gāṃ dvihāyanīṃ rohiṇīm ekarūpāṃ bandhayati
9.1.3	niśi śāmūlaparihito jyeṣṭho 'nvālabhate
9.1.4	patny ahatavasanā jyeṣṭham
9.1.5	patnīm anvañca itare
9.1.6	athainān abhivyāhārayaty adhrigo śamīdhvam / suśami śamīdhvam / śamīdhvam adhrigā o u iti triḥ
9.1.7	ayam agniḥ satpatir naḍam ā rohety anuvākaṃ mahāśāntiṃ ca śāntyudaka āvapate
9.1.8	agne akravyād iti bhraṣṭrād dīpaṃ dhārayati
9.1.9	bhūmeś copadagdhaṃ samutkhāya
9.1.10	ākṛtiloṣṭavalmīkenāstīrya
9.1.11	śakṛtpiṇḍenābhilipya
9.1.12	sikatābhiḥ prakīryābhyukṣya
9.1.13	lakṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā
9.1.14	punar abhyukṣya
9.1.15	paścāl lakṣaṇasyābhimanthanaṃ nidhāya
9.1.16	go'śvājāvīnāṃ puṃsāṃ lomabhir āstīrya vrīhiyavaiś ca śakṛtpiṇḍam abhivimṛjya prāñcau darbhau nidadhāti
9.1.17	vṛṣaṇau stha ity abhiprāṇyāraṇyau
9.1.18	tayor uparyadharāraṇim
9.1.19	dakṣiṇato mūlān
9.1.20	paścāt prajananām urvaśy asīty āyur asīti
9.1.21	mūlata uttarāraṇim upasaṃdhāya
9.1.22	pṛtanājitam ity āhūya
9.1.23	abhidakṣiṇaṃ jyeṣṭhas trir abhimanthaty oṃ bhūr gāyatraṃ chando 'nuprajāyasva traiṣṭubhaṃ jāgatam ānuṣṭubham oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar janad om iti
9.1.24	ata ūrdhvaṃ yathākāmam
9.2.1	manthāmi tvā jātavedaḥ sujātaṃ jātavedasam / sa no jīveṣv ā bhaja dīrgham āyuś ca dhehi naḥ / jāto 'janiṣṭhā yaśasā sahāgre prajāṃ paśūṃs tejo rayim asmāsu dhehi / ānandino modamānāḥ suvīrā anāmayāḥ sarvam āyur gamema / uddīpyasva jātavedo 'va sediṃ tṛṣṇāṃ kṣudhaṃ jahi / apāsmat tama ucchatv apa hrītamukho jahy apa durhārddiśo jahi / ihaivaidhi dhanasanir iha tvā samidhīmahi / ihaidhi puṣṭivardhana iha tvā samidhīmahīti
9.2.2	prathamayā manthati
9.2.3	dvitīyayā jātam anumantrayate
9.2.4	tṛtīyayoddīpayati
9.2.5	caturthyopasamādadhāti
9.2.6	yat tvā kruddhā iti coṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar janad om ity aṅgirasāṃ tvā devānām ādityānāṃ vratenādadhe / dyaur mahnāsi bhūmir bhūmnā tasyās te devy aditir upasthe 'nnādāyānnapatyāyādadhad iti
9.2.7	lakṣaṇe pratiṣṭhāpyopotthāya
9.2.8	athopatiṣṭhate
9.2.9	agne gṛhapate sugṛhapatir ahaṃ tvayāgne gṛhapatinā bhūyāsam / sugṛhapatis tvaṃ mayāgne gṛhapatinā bhūyāḥ / asthūri ṇau gārhapatyāni dīdihi śataṃ samā iti
9.2.10	vyākaromīti gārhapatyakravyādau samīkṣate
9.2.11	śāntam ājyaṃ gārhapatyāyopanidadhāti
9.2.12	māṣamanthaṃ kravyādam
9.2.13	upa tvā namaseti puronuvākyā
9.2.14	viśvahā ta iti pūrṇāhutiṃ juhoti
9.2.15	yo no agnir iti saha kartrā hṛdayānyabhimṛśante
9.3.1	aṃśo rājā vibhajatīmāv agnī vidhārayan / kravyādaṃ nirṇudāmasi havyavāḍ iha tiṣṭhatv iti vibhāgaṃ japati
9.3.2	sugārhapatya iti dakṣiṇena gārhapatye samidham ādadhāti
9.3.3	yaḥ kravyāt tam aśīśamam iti savyena naḍamayīṃ kravyādi
9.3.4	apāvṛtyeti mantroktaṃ bāhyato nidhāya
9.3.5	naḍam ā roha sam indhata iṣīkāṃ jaratīṃ pratyañcam arkam ity upasamādadhāti
9.3.6	yady agnir yo agnir aviḥ kṛṣṇā / mā no ruroḥ śucadvidaḥ śivo no astu bharato rarāṇaḥ / ativyādhī vyādho agrabhīṣṭa kravyādo agnīñ śamayāmi sarvān iti śuktyā māṣapiṣṭāni juhoti
9.3.7	sīsaṃ darvyām avadhāyodgrathya manthaṃ juhvañśamayet
9.3.8	naḍam ā roheti catasro 'gne akravyād imaṃ kravyād yo no aśveṣv anyebhyas tvā hiraṇyapāṇim iti śamayati
9.3.9	dakṣiṇato jaratkoṣṭhe śītaṃ bhasmābhiviharati
9.3.10	śāntyudakena suśāntaṃ kṛtvāvadagdhaṃ samutkhāya
9.3.11	paraṃ mṛtyo ity utthāpayati
9.3.12	kravyādam iti tisṛbhir hrīyamāṇam anumantrayate
9.3.13	dīpādy ābhinigadanāt pratiharaṇena vyākhyātam
9.3.14	aviḥ kṛṣṇeti nidadhāti
9.3.15	uttamavarjaṃ jyeṣṭhasyāñjalau sīsāni
9.3.16	asmin vayaṃ yad ripraṃ sīse mṛḍḍhvam ity abhyavanejayati
9.3.17	kṛṣṇorṇayā pāṇipādān nimṛjya
9.3.18	ime jīvā udīcīnair iti mantroktam
9.3.19	triḥ sapteti kūdyā padāni lopayitvā nadībhyaḥ
9.3.20	mṛtyoḥ padam iti dvitīyayā nāvaḥ
9.3.21	paraṃ mṛtyo iti prāgdakṣiṇam kūdīṃ pravidhya
9.3.22	sapta nadīrūpāṇi kārayitvodakena pūrayitvā
9.3.23	ā rohata savitur nāvam etāṃ sutrāmāṇaṃ mahīm ū ṣv iti sahiraṇyāṃ sayavāṃ nāvam ārohayati
9.3.24	aśmanvatī rīyata ut tiṣṭhatā pra taratā sakhāya ity udīcas tārayati
9.4.1	uttarato garta udakprasravaṇe 'śmānaṃ nidadhāty antaśchinnam
9.4.2	tiro mṛtyum ity aśmānam atikrāmati
9.4.3	tā adharād udīcīr ity anumantrayate
9.4.4	nissālām iti śālāniveśanaṃ samprokṣya
9.4.5	ūrjaṃ bibhrad iti prapādayati
9.4.6	vaiśvadevīm iti vatsatarīm ālambhayati
9.4.7	imam indram iti vṛṣam
9.4.8	anaḍvāham ahorātre iti talpam ālambhayati
9.4.9	ā rohatāyur ity ārohati
9.4.10	āsīnā ity āsīnām anumantrayate
9.4.11	piñjūlīr āñjanaṃ sarpiṣi paryasyemā nārīr iti strībhyaḥ prayacchati
9.4.12	ime jīvā avidhavāḥ sujāmaya iti puṃbhya ekaikasmai tisras tisras tā adhy adhy udadhānaṃ paricṛtya prayacchati
9.4.13	paraṃ mṛtyo vyākaromy ā rohatāntardhiḥ pratyañcam arkaṃ ye agnayo namo devavadhebhyo 'gne 'bhyāvartinn agne jātavedaḥ saha rayyā punar ūrjeti
9.4.14	agne 'bhyāvartinn abhi na ā vavṛtsva / āyuṣā varcasā sanyā medhayā prajayā dhanena / agne jātavedaḥ śataṃ te sahasraṃ ta upāvṛtaḥ / adhā puṣṭasyeśānaḥ punar no rayim ā kṛdhi / saha rayyā ni vartasvāgne pinvasva dhārayā / viśvapsnyā viśvatas pari / punar ūrjā vavṛtsva punar agna iṣāyuṣā / punar naḥ pāhy aṃhasaḥ
9.4.15	śarkarān svayamātṛṇṇāñ śaṇarajjubhyāṃ vibadhya dhārayati
9.4.16	samayā khena juhoti
9.4.17	imaṃ jīvebhya iti dvāre nidadhāti
9.4.18	juhotyetayarcā / āyurdāvā dhanadāvā baladāvā paśudāvā puṣṭidāvā prajāpataye svāheti
9.4.19	ṣaṭsaṃpātaṃ mātā putrān āśayate
9.4.20	ucchiṣṭaṃ jāyām
9.4.21	saṃvatsaram agniṃ nodvāyānna harennāhareyuḥ
9.4.22	dvādaśarātra ity eke
9.4.23	daśa dakṣiṇā
9.4.24	paścād agner vāgyataḥ saṃviśati
9.4.25	aparedyur agniṃ cendrāgnī ca yajeta
9.4.26	sthālīpākābhyām agniṃ cāgniṣomau ca paurṇamāsyām
9.4.27	sāyaṃ prātar vrīhīn āvaped yavān vāgnaye svāhā prajāpataye svāheti sāyam
9.4.28	sūryāya svāhā prajāpataye svāheti prātaḥ
9.4.29	dvādaśarātre 'gniṃ paśunā yajeta
9.4.30	sthālīpākena vobhayor viriṣyati
9.4.31	saṃvatsaratamyāṃ śāntyudakaṃ kṛtvā
9.4.32	ghṛtāhutir no bhavāgne akravyāhutir ghṛtāhutiṃ tvā vayam akravyāhutim upaniṣadema jātaveda iti catura udapātre saṃpātān ānīya
9.4.33	tān ullapya
9.4.34	purastād agneḥ pratyaṅ āsīno juhoti / hute rabhasva hutabhāga edhi mṛḍāsmabhyaṃ mota hiṃsīḥ paśūn na iti
9.4.35	yady udvāyād bhasmanāraṇiṃ saṃspṛśya tūṣṇīṃ mathitvoddīpya
9.4.36	pūrṇahomaṃ hutvā
9.4.37	saṃnatibhir ājyaṃ juhuyād vyāhṛtibhir vā
9.4.38	saṃsṛṣṭe caivaṃ juhuyāt
9.4.39	agnāvanugate jāyamāne
9.4.40	ānaḍuhena śakṛtpiṇḍenāgnyāyatanāni parilipya
9.4.41	homyam upasādya
9.4.42	prāṇāpānābhyāṃ svāhā samānavyānābhyāṃ svāhodānarūpābhyāṃ svāhety ātmany eva juhuyāt
9.4.43	atha prātar utthāyāgniṃ nirmathya yathāsthānaṃ praṇīya yathāpuram agnihotraṃ juhuyāt
9.4.44	sāyamāśaprātarāśau yajñāv ṛtvijau
9.5.1	purodayād astamayāc ca pāvakaṃ prabodhayed gṛhiṇī śuddhahastā / samatīte saṃdhivarṇe 'tha hāvayet susamiddhe pāvaka āhutīṣahiḥ
9.5.2	agnaye ca prajāpataye ca rātrāv ādityaś ca divā prajāpatiś ca / udakaṃ ca samidhaś ca home home puro varam
9.5.3	homyaiḥ samidbhiḥ payasā sthālīpākena sarpiṣā / sāyaṃ prātar homa eteṣām ekenāpi sidhyati
9.5.4	abhyuddhṛto huto 'gniḥ pramādād upaśāmyati / mathite vyāhṛtīr juhuyāt pūrṇahomau yathartvijau
9.5.5	vanaspatibhyo vānaspatyebhya oṣadhibhyo vīrudbhyaḥ sarvebhyo devebhyo devajanebhyaḥ puṇyajanebhya iti prācīnaṃ tad udakaṃ ninīyate
9.5.6	svadhā prapitāmahebhyaḥ svadhā pitāmahebhyaḥ svadhā pitṛbhya iti dakṣiṇataḥ
9.5.7	tārkṣyāyāriṣṭanemaye 'mṛtaṃ mahyam iti paścāt
9.5.8	somāya saptarṣibhya iti uttarataḥ
9.5.9	parimṛṣṭe parilipte ca parvaṇi vrātapataṃ hāvayed annam agnau / bhūyo dattvā svayam alpaṃ ca bhuktvāparāhṇe vratam upaiti yājñikam
9.5.10	anaśanaṃ brahmacaryaṃ ca bhūmau śucir agnim upaśete sugandhiḥ
9.5.11	agnīṣomābhyāṃ darśana indrāgnibhyām adarśane / āgneyaṃ tu pūrvaṃ nityam anvāhāryaṃ prajāpateḥ
9.5.12	ardhāhutis tu sauviṣṭakṛtī sarveṣāṃ haviṣāṃ smṛtā / ānumatī vā bhavati sthālīpākeṣv atharvaṇām
9.5.13	ubhau ca saṃdhijau yau vaiśvadevau yathartvijau / varjayitvā sabarhiṣaḥ sājyā yajñāḥ sadakṣiṇāḥ
9.5.14	yathāśakti yathābalaṃ hutādo 'nye ahutādo 'nye / vaiśvadevaṃ havir ubhaye saṃcaranti / te samyañca iha mādayantām iṣam ūrjaṃ yajamānā yam icchata
9.5.15	viśve devā idaṃ havir ādityāsaḥ saparyata / asmin yajñe mā vyathiṣy amṛtāya haviṣkṛtam
9.5.16	vaiśvadevasya haviṣaḥ sāyaṃ prātar juhoti / sāyamāśaprātarāśau yajñāv etau smṛtāv ubhau
9.5.17	apratibhuktau śucikāryau ca nityaṃ vaiśvadevau jānatā yajñaśreṣṭhau / nāśrotriyo nānavaniktapāṇir nāmantravij juhuyān nāvipaścit
9.5.18	bībhatsavaḥ śucikāmā hi devā nāśraddadhānasya havir juṣante / brāhmaṇena brahmavidā tu hāvayen na strīhutaṃ śūdrahutaṃ ca devagam
9.5.19	yas tu vidyād ājyabhāgau yajñān mantraparikramān / devatājñānam āvṛta āśiṣaś ca karma striyā apratiṣiddham āhuḥ
9.6.1	tayor baliharaṇam
9.6.2	agnaya indrāgnibhyāṃ vāstoṣpataye prajāpataye 'numataya iti hutvā
9.6.3	niṣkramya bahiḥ prācīnaṃ brahmaṇe vaiśravaṇāya viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ sarvebhyo devebhyo viśvebhyo bhūtebhyaḥ sarvebhyo bhūtebhya iti bahuśo baliṃ haret
9.6.4	dviḥ prokṣan pradakṣiṇam āvṛtyāntarupātītya dvāre
9.6.5	dvāryayor mṛtyave dharmādharmābhyām
9.6.6	udadhāne dhanvantaraye samudrāyauṣadhivanaspatibhyo dyāvāpṛthivībhyām iti
9.6.7	sthūṇāvaṃśayor digbhyo 'ntardeśebhya iti

9.6.11	bhūyo 'bhyuddhṛtya brāhmaṇān bhojayet
9.6.12	tad api śloko vadati / mā brāhmaṇāgrataḥ kṛtam aśnīyād viṣavad annam annakāmyā / devānāṃ devo brāhmaṇo bhāvo nāmaiṣa devateti
9.6.13	āgrayaṇe śāntyudakaṃ kṛtvā yathartu taṇḍulān upasādya
9.6.14	apsu sthālīpākaṃ śrapayitvā payasi vā
9.6.15	sajūr ṛtubhiḥ sajūr vidhābhiḥ sajūr agnaye svāhā / sajūr indrāgnibhyāṃ sajūr dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ sajūr viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ sajūr ṛtubhiḥ sajūr vidhābhiḥ sajūḥ somāya svāhety ekahavir vā syān nānāhavīṃṣi vā
9.6.16	saumyaṃ tanvacchyāmākaṃ śaradi
9.6.17	atha yajamānaḥ prāśitraṃ gṛhṇīte
9.6.18	prajāpateṣ ṭvā grahaṃ gṛhṇāmi / mahyaṃ bhūtyai mahyaṃ puṣṭyai mahyaṃ śriyai mahyaṃ hriyai mahyaṃ yaśase mahyam āyuṣe mahyam annāya mahyam annādyāya mahyaṃ sahasrapoṣāya mahyam aparimitapoṣāyeti
9.6.19	atha prāśnāti / bhadrān naḥ śreyaḥ samanaiṣṭa devās tvayāvasena samaśīmahi tvā / sa naḥ pito madhumāṁ āviveśa śivas tokāya tanvo na ehīti
9.6.20	prāśitam anumantrayate / amo 'si prāṇa tad ṛtaṃ bravīmy amāsi sarvāṅ asi praviṣṭaḥ / sa me jarāṃ rogam apanudya śarīrād anāmayaidhi mā riṣāma indo iti

11.2.33	mainam agne vi dahaḥ śaṃ tapā rabhasva prajānanta iti kaniṣṭha ādīpayati
11.2.34	ādīpte sruveṇa yāmān homāñjuhoti pareyivāṃsaṃ pravato mahīr iti
11.2.35	yamo no gātuṃ prathamo vivedeti dve prathame
11.2.36	aṅgiraso naḥ pitaro navagvā iti saṃhitāḥ sapta
11.2.37	yo mamāra prathamo martyānāṃ ye naḥ pituḥ pitaro ye pitāmahā ity ekādaśa
11.2.38	atha sārasvatāḥ
11.2.39	sarasvatīṃ devayanto havante sarasvatīṃ pitaro havante sarasvati yā sarathaṃ yayātha sarasvati vrateṣu ta idaṃ te havyaṃ ghṛtavat sarasvatīndro mā marutvān iti
11.2.40	dakṣiṇato 'nyasminn anuṣṭhātā juhoti
11.2.41	sarvair upatiṣṭhanti trīṇi prabhṛtir vā
11.2.42	api vānuṣṭhānībhiḥ
11.2.43	etā anuṣṭhānyaḥ
11.2.44	mainam agne vi daha itiprabhṛty ava sṛjeti varjayitvā sahasranīthā ity ātaḥ
11.2.45	ā roha janitrīṃ jātavedasa iti pañcadaśabhir āhitāgnim
11.2.46	mitrāvaruṇā pari mām adhātām iti pāṇī prakṣālayate
11.2.47	varcasā mām ity ācāmati
11.2.48	vivasvān na ity uttarato 'nyasminn anuṣṭhātā juhoti
11.3.1	yavīyaḥprathamāni karmāṇi prāṅmukhānāṃ yajñopavītināṃ dakṣiṇāvṛtām

11.3.3	tāsām ekaikāṃ savyenāvācīnahastenāvakiranto 'navekṣamāṇā vrajanti

11.3.12	śāmyākīḥ samidha ādhāyāgrato brahmā japati

11.3.14	nissālām iti śālāniveśanaṃ samprokṣya

11.3.18	khalvakāsyeti khalvān khalakulāṃśca
11.3.19	vyapādyābhyāṃ śāmyākīr ādhāpayati
11.3.20	tāsāṃ dhūmaṃ bhakṣayanti
11.3.21	yadyat kravyād gṛhyed yadi kravyādā nānte 'paredyuḥ / divo nabhaḥ śukraṃ payo duhānā iṣam ūrjaṃ pinvamānāḥ / apāṃ yonim apādhvaṃ svadhā yāś cakṛṣe jīvaṃs tās te santu madhuścuta ity agnau sthālīpākaṃ nipṛṇāti
11.3.22	ādahane cāpivānyavatsāṃ dohayitvā tasyāḥ pṛṣṭhe juhoti vaiśvānare havir idaṃ juhomīti
11.3.23	tasyāḥ payasi
11.3.24	sthālīpāka ity eke

11.3.26	upa dyāṃ śaṃ te nīhāra iti mantroktānyavadāya
11.3.27	kṣīrotsiktena brāhmaṇasyāvasiñcati madhūtsiktena kṣatriyasyodakena vaiśyasya
11.3.28	ava sṛjety anumantrayate

11.3.30	prathamaṃ śīrṣakapālāni

11.3.32	mā tvā vṛkṣa iti vṛkṣamūle nidadhāti
11.3.33	syonāsmai bhaveti bhūmau trirātram arasāśinaḥ karmāṇi kurvate
11.3.34	daśarātra ity eke
11.3.35	yathākuladharmaṃ vā

11.4.1	pitṝn nidhāsyan saṃbhārān saṃbharati

11.4.16	grāme yāmasārasvatān homān hutvā

11.4.21	avidanto deśāt pāṃsūn

11.8.4	varcasā mām ity ācāmati
11.8.5	punaḥ savyenācamanād apasavyaṃ kṛtvā praiṣakṛtaṃ samādiśati
11.8.6	ulūkhalamusalaṃ śūrpaṃ caruṃ kaṃsaṃ prakṣālaya barhir udakumbham ā hareti
11.8.7	yajñopavītī dakṣiṇapūrvam antardeśam abhimukhaḥ śūrpa ekapavitrāntarhitān haviṣyān nirvapati
11.8.8	idam agnaye kavyavāhanāya svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ pṛthiviṣadbhya itīdaṃ somāya pitṛmate svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ somavadbhyaḥ pitṛbhyo vāntarikṣasadbhya itīdaṃ yamāya pitṛmate svadhā pitṛbhyaś ca diviṣadbhya iti trīn avācīnakāśīn nirvapati

11.8.13	śirograhaṃ paricakṣate

11.8.15	avāgaṅguriṃ parvamātrīm ity eke

11.8.23	saṃbhārān upasādayati
11.8.24	paryukṣaṇīṃ barhir udakumbhaṃ kaṃsaṃ darvim ājyam āyavanaṃ caruṃ vāsāṃsy āñjanam abhyañjanam iti
11.8.25	yad atropasamāhāryaṃ bhavati tad upasamāhṛtya
11.8.26	ato yajñopavītī pitryupavītī barhir gṛhītvā vicṛtya saṃnahanaṃ dakṣiṇāparam aṣṭamadeśam abhyavāsyet
11.8.27	barhir udakena samprokṣya barhiṣadaḥ pitara upahūtā naḥ pitaro 'gniṣvāttāḥ pitaro ye naḥ pituḥ pitaro ye 'smākam iti prastṛṇāti
11.8.28	āyāpanādīni trīṇi
11.8.29	ud īratām iti tisṛbhir udapātrāṇyanvṛcaṃ ninayet
11.8.30	ataḥ pitryupavītī yajñopavītī ye dasyava ity ubhayata ādīptam ulmukaṃ triḥ prasavyaṃ parihṛtya nirasyati
11.8.31	paryukṣya
11.9.1	ye rūpāṇi pratimuñcamānā asurāḥ santaḥ svadhayā caranti / tvaṃ tān agne apa sedha dūrān satyāḥ naḥ pitṝṇāṃ santv āśiṣaḥ svāhā svadheti hutvā kumbhīpākam abhighārayati
11.9.2	agnaye kavyavāhanāyeti juhoti
11.9.3	yathāniruptaṃ dvitīyām
11.9.4	yamāya pitṛmate svadhā pitṛbhya iti tṛtīyām
11.9.5	yad vo agnir iti sāyavanāṃs taṇḍulān
11.9.6	saṃ barhir iti sadarbhāṃs taṇḍulān paryukṣya
11.9.7	ato yajñopavītī pitryupavītī darvyoddharati
11.9.8	dyaur darvir akṣitāparimitānupadastā sā yathā dyaur darvir akṣitāparimitānupadastaivā pratatāmahasyeyaṃ darvir akṣitāparimitānupadastā
11.9.9	antarikṣaṃ darvir akṣitāparimitānupadastā sā yathāntarikṣam darvir akṣitāparimitānupadastaivā tatāmahasyeyaṃ darvir akṣitāparimitānupadastā
11.9.10	pṛthivī darvir akṣitāparimitānupadastā sā yathā pṛthivī darvir akṣitāparimitānupadastaivā tatasyeyaṃ darvir akṣitāparimitānupadasteti
11.9.11	uddhṛtyājyena saṃnīya trīn piṇḍān saṃhatān nidadhāty etat te pratatāmaheti
11.9.12	dakṣiṇataḥ patnībhya idaṃ vaḥ patnya iti
11.9.13	idam āśaṃsūnām idam āśaṃsamānānāṃ strīṇāṃ puṃsāṃ prakīrṇāvaśīrṇānāṃ yeṣāṃ vayaṃ dātāro ye cāsmākam upajīvanti / tebhyaḥ sarvebhyaḥ sapatnīkebhyaḥ svadhāvad akṣayyam astv iti triḥ prasavyaṃ taṇḍulaiḥ parikirati
11.9.14	piñjūlīr āñjanaṃ sarpiṣi paryasyāddhvaṃ pitara iti nyasyati
11.9.15	vaddhvaṃ pitaro mā vo 'to 'nyat pitaro yoyuvateti sūtrāṇi
11.9.16	añjate vy añjata ity abhyañjanam
11.9.17	ājyenāvicchinnaṃ piṇḍān abhighārayati ye ca jīvā ye te pūrve parāgatā iti
11.9.18	atra pitaro mādayadhvaṃ yathābhāgaṃ yathālokam āvṛṣāyadhvam iti
11.9.19	atra patnyo mādayadhvaṃ yathābhāgaṃ yathālokam āvṛṣāyadhvam iti
11.9.20	yo 'sāvantaragnir bhavati taṃ pradakṣiṇam avekṣya tisras tāmīs tāmyati
11.9.21	pratiparyāvṛtyāmīmadanta pitaro yathābhāgaṃ yathālokam āvṛṣāyiṣateti
11.9.22	amīmadanta patnyo yathābhāgaṃ yathālokam āvṛṣāyiṣateti
11.9.23	āpo agnim ity adbhir agnim avasicya
11.9.24	putraṃ pautram abhitarpayantīr ity ācāmata mama pratatāmahās tatāmahās tatāḥ sapatnīkās tṛpyantv ācāmantv iti prasavyaṃ pariṣicya
11.9.25	vīrān me pratatāmahā datta vīrān me tatāmahā datta vīrān me pitaro datta pitṝn vīrān yācati
11.9.26	namo vaḥ pitara ity upatiṣṭhati
11.9.27	akṣann ity uttarasicam avadhūya
11.9.28	parā yāteti parāyāpayati
11.9.29	ataḥ pitryupavītī yajñopavītī yan na idaṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha mano 'bhūt tad upāhvayāmīti mana upāhvayati
11.10.1	mano nv āhvāmahe nārāśaṃsena stomena / pitṝṇāṃ ca manmabhiḥ / ā na etu manaḥ punaḥ kratve dakṣāya jīvase / jyok ca sūryaṃ dṛśe / punar naḥ pitaro mano dadātu daivyo janaḥ / jīvaṃ vrātaṃ sacemahi / vayaṃ soma vrate tava manas tanūṣu bibhrataḥ prajāvantaḥ sacemahi / ye sajātāḥ sumanaso jīvā jīveṣu māmakāḥ / teṣāṃ śrīr mayi kalpatām asmin goṣṭhe śataṃ samā iti
11.10.2	yaccarusthālyām odanāvaśiṣṭaṃ bhavati tasyoṣmabhakṣaṃ bhakṣayitvā brāhmaṇāya dadyāt
11.10.3	yadi brāhmaṇo na labhyetāpsv abhyavaharet
11.10.4	nijāya dāsāyety eke
11.10.5	madhyamapiṇḍaṃ patnyai putrakāmāyai prayacchati
11.10.6	ā dhatta pitaro garbhaṃ kumāraṃ puṣkarasrajam / yatheha puruṣo 'sat / ā tvārukṣad vṛṣabhaḥ pṛśnir agriyo medhāvinaṃ pitaro garbham ā dadhuḥ / ā tvāyaṃ puruṣo gamet puruṣaḥ puruṣād adhi / sa te śraiṣṭhyāya jāyatāṃ sa some sāma gāyatv iti
11.10.7	yadyanyā dvitīyā bhavatyaparaṃ tasyai
11.10.8	prāgratamaṃ śrotriyāya
11.10.9	atha yasya bhāryā dāsī vā pradrāviṇī bhavati ye 'mī taṇḍulāḥ prasavyaṃ parikīrṇā bhavanti tāṃs tasyai prayacchati
11.10.10	arvācy upasaṃkrame mā parācy upa vastathā / annaṃ prāṇasya bandhanaṃ tena badhnāmi tvā mayīti
11.10.11	paryukṣaṇīṃ samidhaś cādāya mā pra gāmety āvrajyorjaṃ bibhrad iti gṛhān upatiṣṭhate
11.10.12	ramadhvaṃ mā bibhītanāsmin goṣṭhe karīṣiṇaḥ / ūrjaṃ duhānāḥ śucayaḥ śucivratā gṛhā jīvanta upa vaḥ sadema / ūrjaṃ me devā adadur ūrjaṃ manuṣyā uta / ūrjaṃ pitṛbhya āhārṣam ūrjasvanto gṛhā mama / payo me devā adaduḥ payo manuṣyā uta / payaḥ pitṛbhya āhārṣaṃ payasvanto gṛhā mama / vīryaṃ me devā adaduḥ vīryaṃ manuṣyā uta / vīryaṃ pitṛbhya āhārṣaṃ vīravanto gṛhā mameti
11.10.13	antarupātītya samidho 'bhyādadhāti / ayaṃ no agnir adhyakṣo 'yaṃ no vasuvittamaḥ / asyopasadye mā riṣāmāyaṃ rakṣatu naḥ prajām / asmin sahasraṃ puṣyāsmaidhamānāḥ sve gṛhe / imaṃ sam indhiṣīmahy āyuṣmantaḥ suvarcasaḥ / tvam agna īḍita ā tvāgna indhīmahīti
11.10.14	abhūd dūta ity agniṃ pratyānayati
11.10.15	yadi sarvaḥ praṇītaḥ syād dakṣiṇāgnau tv etad āhitāgneḥ
11.10.16	gṛhyeṣv apy anāhitāgneḥ
11.10.17	idaṃ cin me kṛtam astīdaṃ cicchaknavāni / pitaraś cin mā vedann iti
11.10.18	yo ha yajate taṃ devā vidur yo dadāti taṃ manuṣyā yaḥ śrāddhāni kurute taṃ pitaras taṃ pitaraḥ
12.1.1	madhuparkam āhārayiṣyan darbhān āhārayati
12.1.2	atha viṣṭarān kārayati
12.1.3	sa khalv ekaśākham eva prathamaṃ pādyaṃ dviśākham āsanaṃ triśākhaṃ madhuparkāya
12.1.4	sa yāvato manyeta tāvata upādāya vivicya samparyāpya mūlāni ca prāntāni ca yathāvistīrṇa iva syād ity upotkṛṣya madhyadeśe 'bhisaṃnahyati
12.1.5	ṛtena tvā satyena tvā tapasā tvā karmaṇā tveti saṃnahyati
12.1.6	atha ha sṛjaty atisṛṣṭo dveṣṭā yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
12.1.7	asya ca dātur iti dātāram īkṣate
12.1.8	athodakam āhārayati pādyaṃ bho iti
12.1.9	hiraṇyavarṇābhiḥ pratimantrya dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ prathamaṃ prakarṣati / mayi brahma ca tapaś ca dhārayāṇīti
12.1.10	dakṣiṇe prakṣālite savyaṃ prakarṣati / mayi kṣatraṃ ca viśaś ca dhārayāṇīti
12.1.11	prakṣālitāvanumantrayate / imau pādāv avaniktau brāhmaṇaṃ yaśasāvatām / āpaḥ pādāvanejanīr dviṣantaṃ nir dahantu me
12.1.12	asya ca dātur iti dātāram īkṣate
12.1.13	athāsanam āhārayati / saviṣṭaram āsanam bho iti
12.1.14	tasmin pratyaṅmukha upaviśati
12.1.15	vimṛgvarīṃ pṛthivīm ity etayā viṣṭare pādau pratiṣṭhāpyādhiṣṭhito dveṣṭā yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
12.1.16	asya ca dātur iti dātāram īkṣate
12.1.17	athodakam āhārayatyarghyaṃ bho iti
12.1.18	tat pratimantrayate / annānāṃ mukham asi mukham ahaṃ śreṣṭhaḥ samānānāṃ bhūyāsam / āpo 'mṛtaṃ sthāmṛtaṃ mā kṛṇuta dāsāsmākaṃ bahavo bhavanty aśvāvad goman mayy astu puṣṭam oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar janad om iti
12.1.19	tūṣṇīm adhyātmaṃ ninayati
12.1.20	tejo 'sy amṛtam asīti lalāṭam ālabhate
12.1.21	athodakam āhārayatyācamanīyaṃ bho iti
12.1.22	jīvābhir ācamya
12.1.23	athāsmai madhuparkaṃ vedayante dvyanucaro madhuparko bho iti
12.1.24	dvābhyāṃ śākhābhyām adhastād ekayopariṣṭāt sāpidhānam
12.1.25	madhu vātā ṛtāyata ity etābhir evābhimantraṇam
12.1.26	tathā pratimantraṇam
12.2.1	madhu vātā ṛtāyate madhu kṣaranti sindhavaḥ / mādhvīr gāvo bhavantu naḥ / madhu naktam utoṣaso madhumat pārthivaṃ rajaḥ / mādhvīr naḥ santv oṣadhīḥ / madhumān no vanaspatir madhumāṁ astu sūryaḥ / madhu dyaur astu naḥ pitā
12.2.2	tat sūryasya tvā cakṣuṣā pratīkṣa iti pratīkṣate
12.2.3	ayuto 'ham devasya tvā savitur iti pratigṛhya puromukhaṃ prāgdaṇḍaṃ nidadhāti
12.2.4	pṛthivyās tvā nābhau sādayāmy adityā upastha iti bhūmau pratiṣṭhāpya
12.2.5	dvābhyām aṅgulibhyāṃ pradakṣiṇam ācālyānāmikayāṅgulyāṅguṣṭhena ca saṃgṛhya prāśnāti
12.2.6	oṃ bhūs tat savitur vareṇyaṃ bhūḥ svāheti prathamam
12.2.7	bhargo devasya dhīmahi bhuvaḥ svāheti dvitīyam
12.2.8	dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt svaḥ svāheti tṛtīyam
12.2.9	vayaṃ devasya dhīmahi janat svāheti caturtham
12.2.10	turaṃ devasya bhojanaṃ vṛdhat svāheti pañcamam
12.2.11	karat svāheti ṣaṣṭham
12.2.12	ruhat svāheti saptamam
12.2.13	mahat svāhety aṣṭamam
12.2.14	tat svāheti navamam
12.2.15	śaṃ svāheti daśamam
12.2.16	om iti ekādaśam
12.2.17	tūṣṇīṃ dvādaśam
12.2.18	tasya bhūyomātram iva bhuktvā brāhmaṇāya śrotriyāya prayacchet
12.2.19	śrotriyālābhe vṛṣalāya prayacchet
12.2.20	athāpy ayaṃ nigamo bhavati / somam etat pibata yat kiṃ cāśnīta brāhmaṇāḥ / mābrāhmaṇāyocchiṣṭaṃ dāta mā somaṃ pātv asomapa iti
12.3.1	dadhi ca madhu brāhmo madhuparkaḥ
12.3.2	pāyasa aindro madhuparkaḥ
12.3.3	madhu cājyaṃ ca saumyo madhuparkaḥ
12.3.4	manthaś cājyaṃ ca pauṣṇo madhuparkaḥ
12.3.5	kṣīraṃ cājyaṃ ca sārasvato madhuparkaḥ
12.3.6	surā cājyaṃ ca mausalo madhuparkaḥ
12.3.7	sa khalv eṣa dvaye bhavati sautrāmaṇyāṃ ca rājasūye ca
12.3.8	udakaṃ cājyaṃ ca vāruṇo madhuparkaḥ
12.3.9	tailaṃ cājyaṃ ca śrāvaṇo madhuparkaḥ
12.3.10	tailaś ca piṇḍaś ca pārivrājako madhuparkaḥ
12.3.11	iti khalv eṣa navavidho madhuparko bhavati
12.3.12	athāsmai gāṃ vedayante gaur bho iti
12.3.13	tān pratimantrayate / bhūtam asi bhavad asy annaṃ prāṇo bahur bhava / jyeṣṭhaṃ yan nāma nāmata oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar janad om iti
12.3.14	atisṛjati / mātādityānāṃ duhitā vasūnāṃ svasā rudrāṇām amṛtasya nābhiḥ / pra ṇo vocaṃ cikituṣe janāya mā gām anāgām aditiṃ vadhiṣṭa / oṃ tṛṇāni gaur attv iti āha
12.3.15	sūyavasād iti pratiṣṭhamānām anumantrayate
12.3.16	nālohito madhuparko bhavati
12.3.17	nānujñānam adhīmaha iti kurutety eva brūyāt
12.3.18	svadhite mainaṃ hiṃsīr iti śastraṃ prayacchati
12.3.19	pāpmānaṃ me 'pa jahīti kartāram anumantrayate
12.3.20	āgneyīṃ vapāṃ kuryuḥ
12.3.21	api vā brāhmaṇa eva prāśnīyāt taddevataṃ hi taddhavir bhavati
12.3.22	athāsmai snānam anulepanaṃ mālābhyañjanam iti
12.3.23	yad atropasamāhāryaṃ bhavati tad upasamāhṛtya
12.3.24	athopāsakāḥ prāyopāsakāḥ smo bho iti vedayante
12.3.25	tān pratimantrayate / bhūyāṃso bhūyāsma ye ca no bhūyasaḥ kārṣṭāpi ca no 'nye bhūyāṃso jāyantām
12.3.26	asya ca dātur iti dātāram īkṣate
12.3.27	athānnāhārāḥ prāpyānnāhārāḥ smo bho iti vedayante
12.3.28	tān pratimantrayate / annādā bhūyāsma ye ca no 'nnādān kārṣṭāpi ca no 'nye 'nnādā bhūyāṃso jāyantām
12.3.29	asya ca dātur iti dātāram īkṣate
12.3.30	āhṛte 'nne juhoti yat kāma kāmayamānā ity etayā
12.3.31	yat kāma kāmayamānā idaṃ kṛṇmasi te haviḥ / tan naḥ sarvaṃ samṛdhyatām athaitasya haviṣo vīhi svāheti
12.3.32	eṣa ācāryakalpa eṣa ṛtvikkalpa eṣa saṃyuktakalpa eṣa vivāhakalpa eṣo 'tithikalpa eṣo 'tithikalpaḥ

13.2.1	atha yatraitāni varṣāṇi varṣanti ghṛtaṃ māṃsaṃ madhu ca yaddhiraṇyaṃ yāni cāpyanyāni ghorāṇi varṣāṇi varṣanti tat parābhavati kulaṃ vā grāmo vā janapado vā
13.2.2	tatra rājā bhūmipatir vidvāṃsaṃ brahmāṇam icchet
13.2.3	eṣa ha vai vidvān yad bhṛgvaṅgirovit
13.2.4	ete ha vā asya sarvasya śamayitāraḥ pālayitāro yad bhṛgvaṅgirasaḥ
13.2.5	sa āhopakalpayadhvam iti
13.2.6	tad upakalpayante kaṃsamahate vasane śuddham ājyaṃ śāntā oṣadhīr navam udakumbham
13.2.7	trīṇi parvāṇi karmaṇaḥ paurṇamāsyamāvāsye puṇyaṃ nakṣatram
13.2.8	api ced eva yadā kadācid ārtāya kuryāt
13.2.9	snāto 'hatavasanaḥ surabhir vratavān karmaṇya upavasatyekarātraṃ trirātraṃ ṣaḍrātraṃ dvādaśarātraṃ vā
13.2.10	dvādaśyāḥ prātar yatraivādaḥ patitaṃ bhavati tata uttaram agnim upasamādhāya
13.2.11	parisamuhya paryukṣya paristīrya barhir udapātram upasādya paricaraṇenājyaṃ paricarya
13.2.12	nityān purastāddhomān hutvājyabhāgau ca
13.2.13	atha juhoti
13.2.14	ghṛtasya dhārā iha yā varṣanti pakvaṃ māṃsaṃ madhu ca yaddhiraṇyam / dviṣantam etā anuyantu vṛṣṭayo 'pāṃ vṛṣṭayo bahulāḥ santu mahyam / lohitavarṣaṃ madhupāṃsuvarṣaṃ yad vā varṣaṃ ghoram aniṣṭam anyat / dviṣantam ete anuyantu sarve parāñco yantu nirvartamānāḥ / agnaye svāheti hutvā
13.2.15	divyo gandharva iti mātṛnāmabhir juhuyāt

13.2.17	sīraṃ vaiśyo 'śvaṃ prādeśiko grāmavaraṃ rājā
13.2.18	sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ
13.3.1	atha yatraitāni yakṣāṇi dṛśyante tad yathaitanmarkaṭaḥ śvāpado vāyasaḥ puruṣarūpam iti tad evam āśaṅkyam eva bhavati
13.3.2	tatra juhuyāt
13.3.3	yan markaṭaḥ śvāpado vāyaso yadīdaṃ rāṣṭraṃ jātavedaḥ patāti puruṣarakṣasaṃ iṣiraṃ yat patāti / dviṣantam ete anuyantu sarve parāñco yantu nivartamānāḥ / agnaye svāheti hutvā
13.3.4	divyo gandharva iti mātṛnāmabhir juhuyāt

13.4.1	atha ha gomāyū nāma maṇḍūkau yatra vadatas tad yanmanyante māṃ prati vadato māṃ prati vadata iti tad evam āśaṅkyam eva bhavati
13.4.2	tatra juhuyāt
13.4.3	yad gomāyū vadato jātavedo 'nyayā vācābhijañjabhātaḥ / rathaṃtaraṃ bṛhac ca sāmaitad dviṣantam etāv abhinānadaitām / rathaṃtareṇa tvā bṛhacchamayāmi bṛhatā tvā rathantaraṃ śamayāmi / indrāgnī tvā brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānāvāyuṣmantāvuttamaṃ tvā karāthaḥ / indrāgnibhyāṃ svāheti hutvā
13.4.4	divyo gandharva iti mātṛnāmabhir juhuyāt
13.4.5	sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ
13.5.1	atha yatraitat kulaṃ kalahi bhavati tan nirṛtigṛhītam ity ācakṣate
13.5.2	tatra juhuyāt
13.5.3	ārād arātim iti dve
13.5.4	ayāś cāgne 'sy anabhiśastiś ca satyam it tvam ayā asi / ayāsā manasā kṛto 'yās san havyam ūhiṣe / ā no dhehi bheṣajam / svāhety agnau hutvā
13.5.5	tatraivaitān homāñ juhuyāt
13.5.6	ārād agniṃ kravyādaṃ nirūhañ jīvātave te paridhiṃ dadhāmi / indrāgnī tvā brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānāv āyuṣmantāv uttamaṃ tvā karāthaḥ / indrāgnibhyāṃ svāheti hutvā
13.5.7	apeta etu nirṛtir ity anena sūktena juhuyāt
13.5.8	apeta etu nirṛtir nehāsyā api kiṃcana / apāsyāḥ satvanaḥ pāśān mṛtyūn ekaśataṃ nude / ye te pāśā ekaśataṃ mṛtyo martyāya hantave / tāṃs te yajñasya māyayā sarvān apayajāmasi / nir ito yantu nairṛtyā mṛtyava ekaśatam / paraḥ sedhāmaiṣāṃ yat tamaḥ prāṇaṃ jyotiś ca dadhmahe / ye te śataṃ varuṇa ye sahasraṃ yajñiyāḥ pāśā vitatā mahāntaḥ / tebhyo asmān varuṇaḥ soma indro viśve muñcantu marutaḥ svarkāḥ / brahma bhrājad udagād antarikṣaṃ divaṃ ca brahmāvādhūṣṭāmṛtena mṛtyum / brahmopadraṣṭā sukṛtasya sākṣād brahmāsmad apahantu śamalaṃ tamaś ca

13.14.7	kumudvatī puṣkariṇī sītā sarvāṅgaśobhanī / kṛṣiḥ sahasraprakārā pratyaṣṭā śrīr iyaṃ mayi / urvīṃ tvāhur manuṣyāḥ śriyaṃ tvā manaso viduḥ / āśaye 'nnasya no dhehy anamīvasya śuṣmiṇaḥ / parjanyapatni hariṇyabhijitāsy abhi no vada / kālanetre haviṣo no juṣasva tṛptiṃ no dhehi dvipade catuṣpade / yābhir devā asurān akalpayan yātūn manūn gandharvān rākṣasāṃś ca / tābhir no adya sumanā upāgahi sahasrāpoṣaṃ subhage rarāṇā / hiraṇyasrakpuṣkariṇī śyāmā sarvāṅgaśobhanī / kṛṣir hiraṇyaprakārā pratyaṣṭā śrīr iyaṃ mayi / aśvibhyāṃ devi saha saṃvidānā indreṇa rādhena saha puṣṭyā na āgahi / viśas tvā rāsantāṃ pradiśo 'nu sarvā ahorātrārdhamāsamāsā ārtavā ṛtubhiḥ saha / bhartrī devānām uta martyānāṃ bhartrī prajānām uta mānuṣāṇām / hastibhir itarāsaiḥ kṣetrasārathibhiḥ saha / hiraṇyair aśvair ā gobhiḥ pratyaṣṭā śrīr iyaṃ mayi

13.15.2	manāyai tantuṃ prathamaṃ paśyed anyā atanvata / tan nārīḥ prabravīmi vaḥ sādhvīr vaḥ santūrvarīḥ / sādhur vas tantur bhavatu sādhur etu ratho vṛtaḥ / atho horvarīr yūyaṃ prātar voḍhave dhāvata / khargalā iva patvarīr apām ugram ivāyanam / patantu patvarīr ivorvarīḥ sādhunā pathā / apācyau te totudyete todenāśvatarāv iva / pra stomam urvarīṇāṃ śaśayānām astāviṣam / nārī pañcamayūkhaṃ sūtravat kṛṇute vasu / ariṣṭo asya vastā prendra vāsa utodira

13.24.1	atha yatraitat pipīlikā anācārarūpā dṛśyante tatra juhuyāt

13.24.3	yaḥ prācyāṃ diśi śvetapipīlikānāṃ rājā tasmai svāhā / yo dakṣiṇāyāṃ diśi kṛṣṇapipīlikānāṃ rājā tasmai svāhā / yaḥ pratīcyāṃ diśi rajatapipīlikānāṃ rājā tasmai svāhā / ya udīcyāṃ diśi rohitapipīlikānāṃ rājā tasmai svāhā / yo dhruvāyāṃ diśi babhrupipīlikānāṃ rājā tasmai svāhā / yo vyadhvāyāṃ diśi haritapipīlikānāṃ rājā tasmai svāhā / ya ūrdhvāyāṃ diśy aruṇapipīlikānāṃ rājā tasmai svāhā

13.33.1	atha yatraitad yūpo virohati tatra juhuyāt
13.33.2	yūpo virohañchataśākho adhvaraḥ samāvṛto mohayiṣyan yajamānasya lokān / vedābhigupto brahmaṇā parivṛto 'tharvabhiḥ śāntaḥ sukṛtām etu lokān / yūpo hy arukṣad dviṣatāṃ vadhāya na me yajño yajamānaś ca riṣyāt / saptarṣīṇāṃ sukṛtāṃ yatra lokas tatremaṃ yajñaṃ yajamānaṃ ca dhehi / vanaspate svāheti hutvā
13.33.3	vanaspatiḥ saha devair na āgann iti juhuyāt

13.34.1	atha yatraitad divolkā patati tad ayogakṣemāśaṅkaṃ bhavatyavṛṣṭyāśaṅkaṃ vā
13.34.2	tatra rājā bhūmipatir vidvāṃsaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vṛṇīyāt
13.34.3	sa vṛto 'raṇyasyārdham abhivrajya tatra dvādaśarātram anuśuṣyet
13.34.4	sa khalu pūrvaṃ navarātram āraṇyaśākamūlaphalabhakṣaś cāthottaraṃ trirātraṃ nānyad udakāt
13.34.5	śvobhūte sapta dhenava upakﾱptā bhavanti śvetā kṛṣṇā rohiṇī nīlā pāṭalā surūpā bahurūpā saptamī
13.34.6	tāsām etad dvādaśarātraṃ saṃdugdhaṃ navanītaṃ nidadhāti
13.34.7	dvādaśyāḥ prātar yatraivāsau patitā bhavati tata uttaram agnim upasamādhāya
13.34.8	parisamūhya paryukṣya paristīrya barhiḥ
13.34.9	athāmuṃ navanītaṃ sauvarṇe pātre vilāpya sauvarṇena sruveṇa rakṣoghnaiś ca sūktair yām āhus tārakaiṣā vikeśītyetena sūktenājyaṃ juhvan
13.34.10	avapatite saṃpātān ānīya saṃsthāpya homān
13.34.11	avapatitaṃ śāntyudakena saṃprokṣya

13.34.13	sīraṃ vaiśyo 'śvaṃ prādeśiko grāmavaraṃ rājā

13.35.1	atha yatraitad dhūmaketuḥ saptarṣīn upadhūpayati tad ayogakṣemāśaṅkam ity uktam
13.35.2	pañca paśavas tāyante vāruṇaḥ kṛṣṇo gaur vājo vāvir vā harir vāyavyo bahurūpo diśyo mārutī meṣyāgneyaḥ prājāpatyaś ca kṣīraudano 'pāṃnaptra udraḥ
13.35.3	uteyaṃ bhūmir iti trir varuṇam abhiṣṭūya
13.35.4	apsu te rājann iti catasṛbhir vāruṇasya juhuyāt
13.35.5	vāyav ārundhi no mṛgān asmabhyaṃ mṛgayadbhyaḥ / sa no nediṣṭham ākṛdhi vāto hi raśanākṛta iti vāyavyasya
13.35.6	āśānām iti diśyasya
13.35.7	prati tyaṃ cārum adhvaraṃ gopīthāya prahūyase / marudbhir agna āgahīti mārutasya

13.35.9	prajāpatiḥ salilād iti prājāpatyasya

13.35.11	pra haiva varṣati

13.36.1	atha yatraitannakṣatrāṇi patāpatānīva bhavanti tatra juhuyāt
13.36.2	yan nakṣatraṃ patati jātavedaḥ somena rājñeṣiraṃ purastāt / tasmān mām agne paripāhi ghorāt pra ṇo jāyantāṃ mithunāni rūpaśaḥ / indrāgnibhyāṃ svāheti hutvā
13.36.3	somo rājā savitā ca rājety etena sūktena juhuyāt
13.36.4	somo rājā savitā ca rājā bhuvo rājā bhuvanaṃ ca rājā / śarvo rājā śarma ca rājā ta u naḥ śarma yacchantu devāḥ / ādityair no bṛhaspatir bhagaḥ somena naḥ saha / viśve devā urv antarikṣaṃ ta u naḥ śarma yacchantu devāḥ / utāvidvān niṣkṛdayāthosraghnī yathāyatham / mā no viśve devā maruto hetim icchata

13.37.1	atha yatraitanmāṃsamukho nipatati tatra juhuyāt

13.41.1	atha yatraitad grāmyo 'gniḥ śālāṃ dahaty apamityam apratīttaṃ ity etais tribhiḥ sūktair maiśradhānyasya pūrṇāñjaliṃ hutvā
13.41.2	mamobhā mitrāvaruṇā mahyam āpo madhumad erayantām ity etābhyāṃ sūktābhyāṃ juhuyāt
13.41.3	mamobhā mitrāvaruṇā mamobhendrābṛhaspatī / mama viṣṇuś ca somaś ca mamaiva maruto bhavan / mamobhe dyāvāpṛthivī antarikṣaṃ svar mama / mama gāvo mamāśvā mamājāś cāvayaś ca mamaiva puruṣā bhavan / iti

13.42.1	atha ced āgantur dahatyevam eva kuryāt
13.42.2	sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ
13.43.1	atha yatraitad vaṃśa sphoṭati kapāle 'ṅgārā bhavantyudapātraṃ barhir ājyaṃ tad ādāya
13.43.2	śālāyāḥ pṛṣṭham upasarpati
13.43.3	tatrāṅgārān vā kapālaṃ vopanidadhāty ā saṃtapanāt
13.43.4	prāñcam idhmam upasamādhāya
13.43.5	parisamuhya paryukṣya paristīrya barhir udapātram upasādya
13.43.6	paricaraṇenājyaṃ paricarya
13.43.7	nityān purastāddhomān hutvājyabhāgau ca
13.43.8	atha juhoti
13.43.9	asau vai nāma te mātāsau vai nāma te pitā / asau vai nāma te dūtaḥ svavaṃśam adhitiṣṭhati / uttamarātrī nāma mṛtyo te mātā tasya te antakaḥ pitā / samaṃdadhānas te dūtaḥ svavaṃśam adhitiṣṭhati / bahavo 'sya pāśā vitatāḥ pṛthivyām asaṃkhyeyā aparyantā anantāḥ / yābhir vaṃśān abhinidadhāti prāṇināṃ yān kāṃścemān prāṇabhṛtāṃ jighāṃsan / sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśaṃ mṛtyave svāhā / bṛhaspatir āṅgiraso brahmaṇaḥ putro viśve devāḥ pradadur viśvam ejat / sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśaṃ bṛhaspataya āṅgirasāya svāhā / yasya te 'nnaṃ na kṣīyate bhūya evopajāyate / yasmai bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca sarvam etat pratiṣṭhitam / sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśam indrāya svāhā / mukhaṃ devānām iha yo babhūva yo jānāti vayunānāṃ samīpe / yasmai hutaṃ devatā bhakṣayanti vāyunetraḥ supraṇītiḥ sunītiḥ / sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśam agnaye svāhā / yaḥ pṛthivyāṃ cyāvayann eti vṛkṣān prabhañjanena rathena saha saṃvidānaḥ / rasān gandhān bhāvayann eti devo mātariśvā bhūtabhavyasya kartā / sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśaṃ vāyave svāhā / brahmacārī carati brahmacaryam ṛcaṃ gāthāṃ brahma paraṃ jigāṃsan / taṃ vighnā anupariyanti sarve ye antarikṣe ye ca divi śritāsaḥ / taṃ viśo anuparyanti sarvāḥ karmāṇi loke parimohayanti / sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśam ādityāya svāhā / yo nakṣatraiḥ sarathaṃ yāti devaḥ saṃsiddhena rathena saha saṃvidānaḥ / rūpaṃ rūpaṃ kṛṇvānaś citrabhānuḥ subhānuḥ / sa imaṃ dūtaṃ nudatu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśaṃ candrāya svāhā / oṣadhayaḥ somarājñīr yaśasvinīḥ / tā imaṃ dūtaṃ nudantu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśam oṣadhībhyaḥ somarājñībhyaḥ svāhā / oṣadhayo varuṇarājñīr yaśasvinīḥ / tā imaṃ dūtaṃ nudantu vaṃśapṛṣṭhāt sa me gacchatu dviṣato niveśam oṣadhībhyo varuṇarājñībhyaḥ svāhā / aṣṭasthūṇo daśapakṣo yadṛcchajo vanaspate / putrāṃś caiva paśūṃś cābhirakṣa vanaspate / yo vanaspatīnām upatāpo babhūva yad vā gṛhān ghoram utājagāma tan nirjagāma haviṣā ghṛtena śaṃ no astu dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade / yo vanaspatīnām upatāpo na āgād yad vā yajñaṃ no 'dbhutam ājagāma / sarvaṃ tad agne hutam astu bhāgaśaḥ śivān vayam uttaremābhi vājān / tvaṣṭre svāheti hutvā
13.43.10	tvaṣṭā me daivyaṃ vaca ity atrodapātraṃ ninayati
13.43.11	kapāle 'gniṃ cādāyopasarpati
13.43.12	sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ
13.44.1	atha yatraitat kumbhodadhānaḥ saktudhānī vokhā vāniṅgitā vikasati tatra juhuyāt

13.44.3	sadasi san me bhūyād iti saktūn āvapate

14.1.4	apṛthusaṃmitāṃ vediṃ vidadhyāt
14.1.5	ṣaṭśamīṃ prāgāyatāṃ catuḥśamīṃ śroṇyām
14.1.6	trīn madhye ardhacaturthān agrataḥ
14.1.7	trayāṇāṃ purastād uttaravediṃ vidadhyāt

14.1.9	grīṣmas te bhūma ity upasthāya
14.1.10	vi mimīṣva payasvatīm iti mimānam anumantrayate
14.1.11	bṛhaspate pari gṛhāṇa vediṃ sugā vo devāḥ sadanāni santu / asyāṃ barhiḥ prathatāṃ sādhv antarahiṃsrā ṇaḥ pṛthivī devy astv iti parigṛhṇāti
14.1.12	yat te bhūma iti vikhanati

14.1.14	tvam asy āvapanī janānām iti tataḥ pāṃsūn anyatodāhārya
14.1.15	bṛhaspate pari gṛhāṇa vedim ity uttaravedim opyamānāṃ parigṛhṇāti
14.1.16	asaṃbādhaṃ badhyato mānavānām iti prathayati
14.1.17	yasyāś catasraḥ pradiśaḥ pṛthivyā iti caturasrāṃ karoti
14.1.18	devasya tvā savituḥ prasave aśvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyām ā dada iti lekhanam ādāya yatrāgniṃ nidhāsyan bhavati tatra lakṣaṇaṃ karoti

14.1.20	prācīm āvṛtya dakṣiṇataḥ prācīm
14.1.21	aparās tisro madhye
14.1.22	tasyāṃ vrīhiyavāv opya
14.1.23	varṣeṇa bhūmiḥ pṛthivī vṛtāvṛtety adbhiḥ samprokṣya
14.1.24	yasyām annaṃ vrīhiyavāv iti bhūmiṃ namaskṛtya
14.1.25	athāgniṃ praṇayet / tvām agne bhṛgavo nayantām aṅgirasaḥ sadanaṃ śreya ehi / viśvakarmā pura etu prajānan dhiṣṇyaṃ panthām anu te diśāmeti
14.1.26	bhadraśreyaḥsvastyā vā
14.1.27	agne prehīti vā
14.1.28	viśvaṃbharā vasudhānī pratiṣṭheti lakṣaṇe pratiṣṭhāpya
14.1.29	athedhmam upasamādadhāti
14.1.30	agnir bhūmyām oṣadhīṣv agnir diva ā tapaty agnivāsāḥ pṛthivy asitajñūr etam idhmaṃ samāhitaṃ juṣāṇo 'smai kṣatrāṇi dhārayantam agna iti pañcabhi staraṇam
14.1.31	ata ūrdhvaṃ barhiṣaḥ

14.1.34	purastād agner udak saṃstṛṇāti
14.1.35	tathā pratyak
14.1.36	pradakṣiṇaṃ barhiṣāṃ mūlāni chādayantottarasyā vediśroṇeḥ pūrvottarataḥ saṃsthāpya
14.1.37	ahe daidhiṣavyod atas tiṣṭhāny asya sadane sīda yo 'smat pākatara iti brahmāsanam anvīkṣate
14.1.38	nirastaḥ parāgvasuḥ saha pāpmanā nirastaḥ so 'stu yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣma iti dakṣiṇā tṛṇaṃ nirasyati
14.1.39	tad anvālabhya japatīdam aham arvāgvasoḥ sadane sīdāmy ṛtasya sadane sīdāmi satyasya sadane sīdāmīṣṭasya sadane sīdāmi pūrtasya sadane sīdāmi māmṛṣad eva barhiḥ svāsasthaṃ tvādhyāsadeyam ūrṇamradam anabhiśokam
14.1.40	vimṛgvarīm ity upaviśyāsanīyaṃ brahmajapaṃ japati bṛhaspatir brahmā brahmasadana āsiṣyate bṛhaspate yajñaṃ gopāya yad ud udvata un nivataḥ śakeyam
