14.3.1	abhijiti śiṣyān upanīya śvo bhūte saṃbhārān saṃbharati
14.3.2	dadhisaktūn pālāśaṃ daṇḍam ahate vasane śuddham ājyaṃ śāntā oṣadhīr navam udakumbham
14.3.3	bāhyataḥ śāntavṛkṣasyedhmaṃ prāñcam upasamādhāya
14.3.4	parisamuhya paryukṣya paristīrya barhir udapātram upasādya paricaraṇenājyaṃ paricarya
14.3.5	nityān purastāddhomān hutvājyabhāgau ca
14.3.6	paścād agner dadhisaktūñ juhotyagnaye brahmaprajāpatibhyāṃ bhṛgvaṅgirobhya uśanase kāvyāya
14.3.7	tato 'bhayair aparājitair gaṇakarmabhir viśvakarmabhir āyuṣyaiḥ svastyayanair ājyaṃ juhuyāt
14.3.8	mā no devā ahir vadhīd arasasya śarkoṭasyendrasya prathamo ratho yas te sarpo vṛścikas tṛṣṭadaṃśmā namas te astu vidyuta āre 'sāv asmad astu yas te pṛthu stanayitnur iti saṃsthāpya homān
14.3.9	pratiṣṭhāpya sruvaṃ dadhisaktūn prāśyācamyodakam upasamārabhante
14.3.10	avyacasaś ceti japitvā sāvitrīṃ brahma jajñānam ity ekāṃ triṣaptīyaṃ ca paccho vācayet
14.3.11	śeṣam anuvākasya japanti
14.3.12	yo yo bhogaḥ kartavyo bhavati taṃ taṃ kurvate
14.3.13	sa khalv etaṃ pakṣam apakṣīyamāṇaḥ pakṣam adhīyāna upaśrāmyetā darśāt
14.3.14	dṛṣṭe candramasi phalgunīṣu dvayān rasān upasādayati
14.3.15	viśve devā ahaṃ rudrebhiḥ siṃhe vyāghre yaśo havir yaśasaṃ mendro girāv arāgarāṭeṣu yathā somaḥ prātaḥsavane yac ca varco akṣeṣu yena mahānaghnyā jaghanaṃ svāhety agnau hutvā
14.3.16	raseṣu saṃpātān ānīya saṃsthāpya homān
14.3.17	tata etān prāśayati rasān madhu ghṛtāñchiṣyān
14.3.18	yo yo bhogaḥ kartavyo bhavati taṃ taṃ kurvate
14.3.19	nānyata āgatāñ śiṣyān parigṛhṇīyāt parasaṃdīkṣitatvāt
14.3.20	trirātronāṃścaturo māsāñchiṣyebhyaḥ prabrūyād ardhapañcamān vā
14.3.21	pādaṃ pūrvarātre 'dhīyānaḥ pādam apararātre madhyarātre svapan
14.3.22	abhuktvā pūrvarātre 'dhīyāna ity eke
14.3.23	yathāśaktyapararātre duṣparimāṇo ha pādaḥ
14.3.24	pauṣasyāparapakṣe trirātraṃ nādhīyīta
14.3.25	tṛtīyasyāḥ prātaḥ samāsaṃ saṃdiśya yasmāt kośād ity antaḥ
14.3.26	yasmāt kośād udabharāma vedaṃ tasminn antar ava dadhma enam / adhītam iṣṭaṃ brahmaṇo vīryeṇa tena mā devās tapasāvateheti
14.3.27	yo yo bhogaḥ kartavyo bhavati taṃ taṃ kurvate
14.3.28	ye parimokṣaṃ kāmayante te parimucyante
14.4.1	atha rājñām indramahasyopācārakalpaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
14.4.2	proṣṭhapade śuklapakṣe 'śvayuje vāṣṭamyāṃ praveśaḥ
14.4.3	śravaṇenotthāpanam
14.4.4	saṃbhṛteṣu saṃbhāreṣu brahmā rājā cobhau snātāvahatavasanau surabhiṇau vratavantau karmaṇyāv upavasataḥ
14.4.5	śvo bhūte śaṃ no devyāḥ pādair ardharcābhyām ṛcā ṣaṭkṛtvodakam ācāmataḥ
14.4.6	arvāñcam indraṃ trātāram indraḥ sutrāmety ājyaṃ hutvā
14.4.7	athendram utthāpayanti
14.4.8	ā tvāhārṣaṃ dhruvā dyaur viśas tvā sarvā vāñchantv iti sarvato 'pramattā dhārayeran
14.4.9	adbhutaṃ hi vimānotthitam upatiṣṭhante
14.4.10	abhibhūr yajña ity etais tribhiḥ sūktair anvārabdhe rājani pūrṇahomaṃ juhuyāt
14.4.11	atha paśūnām upācāram
14.4.12	indradevatāḥ syuḥ
14.4.13	ye rājño bhṛtyāḥ syuḥ sarve dīkṣitā brahmacāriṇaḥ syuḥ
14.4.14	indraṃ copasadya yajeraṃs trirātraṃ pañcarātraṃ vā
14.4.15	trir ayanam ahnām upatiṣṭhante haviṣā ca yajante
14.4.16	āvṛta indram aham iti
14.4.17	indra kṣatram iti haviṣo hutvā brāhmaṇān paricareyuḥ
14.4.18	na saṃsthitahomāñ juhuyād ity āhur ācāryāḥ
14.4.19	indrasyāvabhṛthād indram avabhṛthāya vrajanti
14.4.20	apāṃ sūktair āplutya pradakṣiṇam āvṛtyāpa upaspṛśyānavekṣamāṇāḥ pratyudāvrajanti
14.4.21	brāhmaṇān bhaktenopepsanti
14.4.22	śvaḥ śvo 'sya rāṣṭraṃ jyāyo bhavatyeko 'syāṃ pṛthivyāṃ rājā bhavati na purā jarasaḥ pramīyate ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān indramaheṇa carati
14.5.1	atha vedasyādhyayanavidhiṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
14.5.2	śrāvaṇyāṃ prauṣṭhapadyāṃ vopākṛtyārdhapañcamān māsān adhīyīran
14.5.3	evaṃ chandāṃsi
14.5.4	lomnāṃ cānivartanam
14.5.5	ardhamāsaṃ copākṛtya kṣaperaṃs tryaham utsṛjya / ārambhaḥ śrāvaṇyām uktaḥ pauṣyām utsarga ucyate
14.5.6	athānadhyāyān vakṣyāmaḥ
14.5.7	brahmajyeṣu nivartate
14.5.8	śrāddhe
14.5.9	sūtakotthānachardaneṣu triṣu caraṇam
14.5.10	ācāryāstamite vā yeṣāṃ ca mānuṣī yoniḥ
14.5.11	yathāśrāddhaṃ tathaiva teṣu
14.5.12	sarvaṃ ca śrāddhikaṃ dravyamadasāhavyapetaṃ pratigṛhyānadhyāyaḥ
14.5.13	prāṇi cāprāṇi ca
14.5.14	dantadhāvane
14.5.15	kṣurasaṃsparśe
14.5.16	prāduṣkṛteṣvagniṣu
14.5.17	vidyutārdharātre stanite
14.5.18	saptakṛtvo varṣeṇa virata ā prātarāśam
14.5.19	vṛṣṭe
14.5.20	nirghāte
14.5.21	bhūmicalane
14.5.22	jyotiṣopasarjana ṛtāv apy ākālam
14.5.23	viṣame na pravṛttiḥ
14.5.24	atha pramāṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ samānaṃ vidyudulkayoḥ / mārgaśīrṣapauṣamāghāparapakṣeṣu tisro 'ṣṭakāḥ
14.5.25	amāvāsyāyāṃ ca
14.5.26	trīṇi cānadhyāni
14.5.27	janane maraṇe caiva daśarātro vidhīyate / ācārye daśarātraṃ syāt sarveṣu ca svayoniṣu
14.5.28	sūtake tv eko nādhīyīta trirātram upādhyāyaṃ varjayet
14.5.29	ācāryaputrabhāryāś ca
14.5.30	atha śiṣyaṃ sahādhyāyinam apradhānaguruṃ copasannam ahorātraṃ varjayet
14.5.31	tathā sabrahmacāriṇaṃ rājānaṃ ca
14.5.32	apartudaivam ākālam
14.5.33	aviśeṣartukālena sarve nirghātādayaḥ smṛtāḥ / yac cānyad daivam adbhutaṃ sarvaṃ nirghātavad bhavet
14.5.34	ṛtāv adhyāyaś chāndasaḥ kālpya āpartukaḥ smṛtaḥ / ṛtāv ūrdhvaṃ prātarāśād yas tu kaścid anadhyāyaḥ / saṃdhyāṃ prāpnoti paścimām
14.5.35	sarveṇa pradoṣo lupyate
14.5.36	niśi nigadāyāṃ ca vidyuti śiṣṭaṃ nādhīyīta
14.5.37	astamite dvisattāyāṃ trisattāyāṃ ca pāṭavaḥ / atha tāvatkālaṃ bhuktvā pradoṣa ubhe saṃdhye
14.5.38	apsu śmaśāne śayyāyām abhiśaste khileṣu ca / antaḥśave rathyāyāṃ grāme cāṇḍālasaṃyute
14.5.39	durgandhe śūdrasaṃśrāve paiṅge śabde bhaye rute / vaidhṛtye nagareṣu ca
14.5.40	aniktena ca vāsasā caritaṃ yena maithunam / śayānaḥ prauḍhapādo cāgratopasthāntike guroḥ
14.5.41	viramya mārute śīghre pratyārambho vibhāṣitaḥ / sarveṇāpararātreṇa viramya pratyārambho na vidyate
14.5.42	pauṣī pramāṇam abhreṣv āpartu ced adhīyānām
14.5.43	varṣaṃ vidyut stanayitnur vā vipadyate
14.5.44	trirātraṃ sthānāsanaṃ brahmacaryam arasāśaṃ copayeyuḥ
14.5.45	sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ
